atha śrīsaṭīkaliṅgamahāpurāṇottarabhāgaprāraṃbhaḥśrīgaṇeśāya namaḥṛṣaya ūcuḥkṛṣṇas tuṣyati keneha sarvadeveśvareśvaraḥ vaktumarhāsi cāsmākaṃ sūta sarvārthavidbhavān  LiP sūta uvācapurā pṛṣṭo mahātejā mārkaṇḍeyo mahāmuniḥ aṃbarīṣeṇa viprendrās tad vadāmi yathātatham  LiP aṃbarīṣa uvācamune samastadharmāṇāṃ pāragas tvaṃ mahāmate mārkaṇḍeya purāṇo si purāṇārthaviśāradaḥ  LiP nārāyaṇānāṃ divyānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ śreṣṭhamuttamam tatkiṃ brūhi mahāprājña bhaktānāmiha suvrata  LiP sūta uvācatasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ smaran nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ kṛṣṇam acyutam avyayam  LiP mārkaṇḍeya uvācaśṛṇu bhūpa yathānyāyaṃ puṇyaṃ nārāyaṇātmakam smaraṇaṃ pūjanaṃ caiva praṇāmo bhaktipūrvakam  LiP pratyekam aśvamedhasya yajñasya samam ucyate ya ekaḥ puruṣaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ paramātmā janārdanaḥ  LiP yasmādbrahmā tataḥ sarvaṃ samāśrityaiva mucyate dharmamekaṃ pravakṣyāmi yaddṛṣṭaṃ viditaṃ mayā  LiP purā tretāyuge kaścit kauśiko nāma vai dvijaḥ vāsudevaparo nityaṃ sāmagānarataḥ sadā  LiP bhojanāsana śayyāsu sadā tadgatamānasaḥ udāracaritaṃ viṣṇor gāyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ  LiP viṣṇoḥ sthalaṃ samāsādya hareḥ kṣetramanuttamam agāyata hariṃ tatra tālavarṇalayānvitam  LiP mūrcchanāsvarayogena śrutibhedena bheditam bhaktiyogaṃ samāpanno bhikṣāmātraṃ hi tatra vai  LiP tatraivaṃ gāyamānaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā kaściddvijastadā padmākhya iti vikhyātastasmai cānnaṃ dadau tadā  LiP sakuṭuṃbo mahātejā hyuṣṇamannaṃ hi tatra vai kauśiko hi tāda hṛṣṭo gāyannāste hariṃ prabhum  LiP śṛṇvannāste sa padmākhyaḥ kāle kāle vinirgataḥ kālayogena saṃprāptāḥ śiṣyā vai kauśikasya ca  LiP sapta rājanyavaiśyānāṃ viprāṇāṃ kulasaṃbhavāḥ jñānavidyādhikāḥ śuddhā vāsudevaparāyaṇāḥ  LiP teṣām api tathānnādyaṃ padmākṣaḥ pradadau svayam śiṣyaiśca sahito nityaṃ kauśiko hṛṣṭamānasaḥ  LiP viṣṇusthale hariṃ tatra āste gāyanyathāvidhi tatraiva mālavo nāma vaiśyo viṣṇuparāyaṇaḥ  LiP dīpamālāṃ harernityaṃ karoti prītimānasaḥ mālavī nāma bhāryā ca tasya nityaṃ pativratā  LiP gomayena samālipya hareḥ kṣetraṃ samantataḥ bhartrā sahāste suprītā śṛṇvatī gānamuttamam  LiP kuśasthalātsamāpannā brāhmaṇāḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ pañcāśadvai samāpannā harergānārthamuttamāḥ  LiP sādhayanto hi kāryāṇi kauśikasya mahātmanaḥ jñānavidyārthatattvajñāḥ śṛṇvanto hyavasaṃstu te  LiP khyātamāsīttadā tasya gānaṃ vai kauśikasya tat śrutvā rājā samabhyetya kaliṅgo vākyamabravīt  LiP kauśikādya gaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ gāyasveha ca māṃ punaḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ ca tathā yūyaṃ kuśasthalajanā api  LiP tacchrutvā kauśikaḥ prāha rājānaṃ sāṃtvayā girā na jihvā me mahārājan vāṇī ca mama sarvadā  LiP hareranyamapindraṃ vā stauti naiva ca vakṣyati evamukte tu tacchiṣyo vāsiṣṭho gautamo hariḥ  LiP sārasvatastathā citraścitramālyastathā śiśuḥ ūcuste pārthivaṃ tadvadyathā prāha ca kauśikaḥ  LiP śravakāste tathā procuḥ pārthivaṃ viṣṇutatparāḥ śrotrāṇīmāni śṛṇvanti hareranyaṃ na pārthiva  LiP gānakīrtiṃ vayaṃ tasya śṛṇumonyāṃ na ca stutim tacchrutvā pārthivo ruṣṭo gāyatāmiti cābravīt  LiP svabhṛtyānbrāhmaṇā hyete kīrtiṃ śṛṇvanti me yathā na śṛṇvanti kathaṃ tasmāt gāyamāne samantataḥ  LiP eva muktāstadā bhṛtyā jaguḥ pārthivamuttamam niruddhamārgā viprāste gāne vṛtte tu duḥkhitāḥ  LiP kāṣṭhasaṃkubhiranyonyaṃ śrotrāṇi vidadhurdvijāḥ kauśikādyāśca tāṃ jñātvā manovṛttiṃ nṛpasya vai  LiP prasahyāsmāṃstu gāyeta svagānesau nṛpaḥ sthitaḥ iti viprāḥ suniyatā jihvāgraṃ cicchiduḥ karaiḥ  LiP tato rājā susaṃkruddhaḥ svadeśāttānnyavāsayat ādāya sarvaṃ vittaṃ ca tataste jagmuruttarām  LiP diśamāsādya kālena kāladharmeṇayojitāḥ tānāgatānyamo dṛṣṭvā kiṃ kartavyamiti sma ha  LiP coṣṭitaṃ tatkṣaṇe rājan brahmā prāha surādhipān kauśikādīn dvijānadya vāsayadhvaṃ yathāsukham  LiP gānayogena ye nityaṃ pūjayanti janārdanam tānānayata bhadraṃ vo yadi devatvamicchatha  LiP ityuktā lokapālaste kauśiketi punaḥ punaḥ mālaveti tathā kecit padmākṣeti tathā pare  LiP krośamānāḥ samabhyetya tānādāya vihāyasā brahmalokaṃ gatāḥ śīghraṃ muhūrtenaiva te surāḥ  LiP kauśikādīṃstato dṛṣṭvā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ pratyudgamya yathānyāyaṃ svāgatenābhyapūjayat  LiP tataḥ kolāhalamabhūdatigauravamulbaṇam brahmaṇā caritaṃ dṛṣṭvā devānāṃ nṛpasattama  LiP hiraṇyagarbho bhagavāṃstānnivārya surottamān kauśikādīnsamādāya munīn devaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ  LiP viṣṇulokaṃ yayau śīghraṃ vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ tatra nārāyaṇodevaḥ śvetadvīpanivāsibhiḥ  LiP jñānayogeśvaraiḥ siddhairviṣṇubhaktaiḥ samāhitaiḥ nārāyaṇasamairdivyaiścaturbāhudharaiḥ śubhaiḥ  LiP viṣṇucihnasamāpannairdīpyamānairakalmaṣaiḥ aṣṭāśītisahasraiśca sevyamāno mahājanaiḥ  LiP asmābhirnāradādyaiśca sanakādyairakalmaṣaiḥ bhūtairnānāvidhaiścaiva divyastrībhiḥ samantataḥ  LiP sevyamānotha madhye vai sahasradvārasaṃvṛte sahasrayojanāyāme divye maṇimaye śubhe  LiP vimāne vimale citre bhadrapīṭhāsane hariḥ lokakārye prasaktānāṃ dattadṛṣṭiśca mādhavaḥ  LiP tasminkāle tha bhagavān kauśikādyaiśca saṃvṛtaḥ āgamya praṇipatyāgre tuṣṭāva garuḍadhvajam  LiP tato kilokya bhagavān harirnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ kauśiketyāha saṃprītyā tānsarvāṃśca yathākramam  LiP jayaghoṣo mahānasīnmahāścarye samāgate brahmāṇamāha viśvātmā śṛṇu brahman mayoditam  LiP kauśikasya ime viprāḥ sādhyasādhanatatparāḥ hitāya saṃpravṛttā vai kuśasthalanivāsinaḥ  LiP matkīrtiśravaṇe yuktā jñānatattvārthakovidāḥ ananyadevatābhaktāḥ sādhyā devā bhavantvime  LiP divyarūpadharaḥ śrīmān śṛṇvangānamihādhipaḥ āsva nityaṃ yathākāmaṃ yāvallokā bhavanti vai  LiP padmākṣamāha bhagavān dhanado bhavamādhavaḥ dhanānāmīśvaro bhūtvā yathākālaṃ hi māṃ punaḥ  LiP mālabaṃ mālavīṃ caivaṃ prāha dāmodaro hariḥ mama loke yathākālaṃ bhāryayā saha mālava  LiP divyarūpadharaḥ śrīmān śṛṇvangānamihādhipaḥ āsva nityaṃ yathākāmaṃ yāvallokā bhavanti vai  LiP padmākṣamāha bhagavān dhanado bhavamādhavaḥ dhanānāmīśvaro bhūtvā yathākālaṃ hi māṃ punaḥ  LiP āgamya dṛṣṭvā māṃ nityaṃ kuru rājyaṃ yathāsukham evamuktvā harirviṣṇurbrahmāṇamidamabravīt  LiP kauśikasyāsya gānena yoganidrā ca me gatā viṣṇusthale ca māṃ stauti śiṣyaireṣa samantataḥ  LiP rājñā nirastaḥ krūreṇa kaliṅgena mahīyasā sa jihvācchedanaṃ kṛtvā hareranyaṃ kathañcana  LiP na stoṣyāmīti niyataḥ prāptosau mama lokatām ete ca viprā niyatā mama bhaktā yaśasvinaḥ  LiP śrotracchidramathāhatya śaṅkubhirvai parasparam śroṣyāmo naiva cānyadvai hareḥ kīrtimitisma ha  LiP ete viprāsca devatvaṃ mama sānnidhyameva ca mālavo bhāryayā sārdhaṃ matkṣetraṃ parimṛjya vai  LiP dīpamālādibhirnityamabhyarcya satataṃ hi mām gānaṃ śṛṇoti niyato matkīrticaritānvitam  LiP tenāsau prāptavāṃllokaṃ mama brahmā sanātanam padmākṣosau dadau bhojyaṃ kauśikasya mahātmanaḥ  LiP dhaneśatvamavāptosau mama sānnidhyameva ca evamuktvā haristatra samāje lokapūjitaḥ  LiP tasmin kṣaṇe samāpannā madhurākṣarapeśalaiḥ vipañcīguṇatattvajñairvādyavidyāviśāradaiḥ  LiP mandaṃ mandasmitā devī vicitrābharaṇānvitā gāyamānā samāyātā lakṣmīrviṣṇuparigrahā  LiP vṛtā sahasrakoṭībhiraṅganābhiḥ samantataḥ tato gaṇādhipā dṛṣṭvā bhuśuṇḍīparighāyudhāḥ  LiP brahmādīṃstarjayantaste munīndevānsamantataḥ utsārayantaḥ saṃhṛṣṭā dhiṣṭhitāḥ parvatopamāḥ  LiP sarve vayaṃ hi niryātāḥ sārdhaṃ vai brahmaṇā suraiḥ tasmin kṣaṇe samāhūtastuṃbarurmunisattamaḥ  LiP praviveśa samīpaṃ vai devyā devasya caiva hi tatrāsīno yathāyogaṃ nānāmūrcchāsamanvitam  LiP jagau kalapadaṃ hṛṣṭo vipañcīṃ cābhyavādayat nānāratnasamāyuktairdivyairābharaṇottamaiḥ  LiP divyamālyaistathā śubhraiḥ pūjito munisattamaḥ nirgatastuṃbarurhṛṣṭo anye ca ṛṣayaḥ surāḥ  LiP dṛṣṭvā saṃpūjitaṃ yāntaṃ yathāyogamarindama nāradotha munirdṛṣṭvā tuṃbaroḥ satkriyāṃ hareḥ  LiP śokāviṣṭena manasā saṃtaptahṛdayekṣaṇaḥ cintāmāpedivāṃstatra śokamūrcchākulātmakaḥ  LiP kenāhaṃ hi haretyāsye yogaṃ devīsamīpataḥ aho tuṃbaruṇā prāptaṃ dhiṅmāṃ mūḍhaṃ vicetasam  LiP yohaṃ hareḥ sannikāśaṃ bhūtairniryātitaḥ katham jīvanyāsyāmi kutrāhamaho tuṃbaruṇā kṛtam  LiP iti saṃcintayan viprastapa āsthitavānmuniḥ divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu nirucchvāsasamanvitaḥ  LiP dhyāyanviṣṇumathādhyāste tuṃbaroḥ satkriyāṃ smaran rodamāno muhurvidvān dhiṅmāmiti ca cintayan  LiP tatra yatkṛtavānviṣṇustacchṛṇuṣva narādhipa  LiP iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge kauśikavṛttakathanaṃ nāma prathamodhyāyaḥmārkaṇḍeya uvācatato nārāyaṇo devastasmai sarvaṃ pradāya vai kālayogena viśvatmā samaṃ cakre tha tuṃbaroḥ  LiP nāradaṃ muniśārdūlamevaṃ vṛttamabhūtpurā nārāyaṇasya gītānāṃ gānaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ punaḥ punaḥ  LiP gānenārādhito viṣṇuḥ satkīrti jñānavarcasī dadāti tuṣṭiṃ sthānaṃ ca yathāsau kauśikasya vai  LiP padmākṣaprabhṛtīnāṃ ca saṃsiddhiṃ pradadau hariḥ tasmāttvayā mahārāja viṣṇukṣatre viśeṣataḥ  LiP arcanaṃ gānanṛtyādyaṃ vādyotsavasamanvitam kartavyaṃ viṣṇubhaktairhi puruṣairaniśaṃ nṛpa  LiP śrotavyaṃ ca sadā nityaṃ śrotavyosau haristathā viṣṇukṣetre tu yo vidvān kārayedbhaktisaṃyutaḥ  LiP gānanṛtyādikaṃ caiva viṣṇvākhyānāṃ kathāṃ tathā jatismṛtiṃ ca medhāṃ ca tathaivoparame smṛtim  LiP prāpnoti viṣṇusāyujyaṃ satyametannṛpādhipa etatte kathitaṃ rājan yanmāṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi  LiP kiṃ vadāmi ca te bhūto vada dharmabhṛtāṃ vara  LiP iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge viṣṇumāhātmyaṃ nāma dvitīyo dhyāyaḥambarīṣa uvācamārkaṇḍeya mahāprājña kena yogena labdhavān gānavidyāṃ mahābhāga nārado bhagavānmuniḥ  LiP tuṃbarośca samānatvaṃ kasminkāla upeyivān etadācakṣva me sarvaṃ sarvajñosi mahāmate  LiP mārkaṇḍeya uvācaśruto mayāyamartho vai nāradāddevadarśanāt svayamahā mahātejā nārado sau mahāmatiḥ  LiP saṃtapyamāno bhagavān divyaṃvarṣasahasrakam nirucchvāsena saṃyuktastuṃbarorgauravaṃ smaran  LiP tatāpa ca mahāghoraṃ taporāśistapaḥ param athāntarikṣe śuśrāva nārado sau mahāmuniḥ  LiP vāṇīṃ divyāṃ mahāghoṣāmadbhutāmasarīriṇīm kimarthaṃ muniśārdūla tapastapasi duścaram  LiP ulūkaṃ paśya gatvā tvaṃ yadi gāne ratā matiḥ mānasottaraśaile tu gānabandhuriti smṛtaḥ  LiP gaccha śīghraṃ ca paśyainaṃ gānavittvaṃ bhaviṣyasi ityukto vismayā viṣṭo nārado vāgvidāṃ varaḥ  LiP mānasottaraśaile tu gānabandhuṃ jagāma vai gandharvāḥ kinnarā yakṣāstathā cāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ  LiP samāsīnāstu parito gānabandhuṃ tatastataḥ ganavidyāṃ samāpannaḥ sikṣitāstena pakṣiṇā  LiP snigdhakaṇṭhasvarās tatra samāsīnām udānvitāḥ tato nāradamālokya gānabandhuruvāca ha  LiP praṇipatya yathānyāyaṃ svāgatenābhyapūjayat kimarthaṃ bhagavānatra cāgato si mahāmate  LiP kiṃ kāryaṃ hi mayā brahman brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi te nārada uvācaulūkendra mahāprājña śṛṇusarvaṃ yathātatham  LiP mama vṛttaṃ pravakṣyāmi purā bhūtaṃ mahādbhutam atīte hi yuge vidvannārāyaṇasamīpagam  LiP māṃ vinirdhūya saṃhṛṣṭaḥ samāhūya ca tuṃbarum lakṣmīsamanvito viṣṇuraśṛṇodgānamuttamam  LiP brahmādayaḥ surāḥ sarve nirastāḥ sthānato cyutāḥ kauśikādyāḥ samāsīnā gānayogena vai harim  LiP evamārādhya saṃprāptā gāṇapatyaṃ yathāsukham tenāhamatiduḥkhārtastapastaptumihāgataḥ  LiP yaddattaṃ yaddhutaṃ caiva yathā vā śrutameva ca yadadhītaṃ mayā sarvaṃ kalāṃ nārhati ṣoḍaśīm  LiP viṣṇormāhātmyayuktasya gāna yogasya vai tataḥ saṃcintyāhaṃ tapo ghoraṃ tadarthaṃ taptavān dvija  LiP divyavarṣasahasraṃ vai tato hyaśṛṇuvaṃ punaḥ vāṇīmākāśasaṃbhūtāṃ tvāmuddiśya vihaṅgama  LiP ulūkaṃ gaccha devaṣe gānabandhuṃ matiryadi gāte cedvartate brahman tatra tvaṃ vetsyase cirāt  LiP ityahaṃ preritastena tvatsamīpamīhāgataḥ kiṃ karīṣyāmi śiṣyohaṃ tava māṃ pālayāvyaya  LiP gānabandhuruvācaśṛṇu nārada yadvṛttaṃ purā mama mahāmate atyāścaryasamāyuktaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ śubham  LiP bhuvaneśa iti khyāto rājabhūddhārmikaḥ purā aśvamedhasahasraiśca vājapeyāyutena ca  LiP gavāṃ koṭyarbude caiva suvarmasya tathaiva ca vāsasāṃ rathahastīnāṃ kanyāśvānāṃ tathaiva ca  LiP datvā sa rājā viprebhyo medinīṃ pratipālayan nivārayan svake rājye geyayogena keśavam  LiP anyaṃ vā geyayogena gāyanyadi sa me bhavet vadhyaḥ sarvātmanā tasmādvedai rīḍyaḥ paraḥ pumān  LiP gānayogena sarvatra striyo gāyantu nityaśaḥ sūtamāgadhasaṃghāśca gītaṃ te kārayantu vai  LiP ityajñāpyamahātejā rājyaṃ vai paryapālayat tasya rājñaḥ purābhyāśe harimitra iti śrutaḥ  LiP brāhmaṇo viṣṇubhaktaśca sarvadvandvavivarjitaḥ nadīpulinamāsādya pratimāṃ ca hareḥ śubhām  LiP abhyarcya ca yathānyāyaṃ ghṛtadadhyuttaraṃ bahu miṣṭānnaṃ pāyasaṃ dattvā harerāvedya pūpakam  LiP praṇipatya yathānyāyaṃ tatra vinyastamānasaḥ agāyata hariṃ tatra tālavarṇalayānvitam  LiP atīva snehasaṃyuktastadgatenāntarātmanā tato rājñaḥ samādeśāccārāstatra samāgatāḥ  LiP tadarcanādi sakalaṃ nirdūya ca samantataḥ brāhmaṇaṃ taṃ gṛhītvā te rājñe samyaṅnyavedayan  LiP tato rājā dvijaśreṣṭhaṃ paribhartsya sudurmatiḥ rājyānnaryātayāmāsa hṛtvā sarvaṃ dhanādikam  LiP pratimāṃ ca hareścaiva mlecchā hṛtvā yayuḥ punaḥ tataḥ kālena mahatā kāladharmamupeyivān  LiP sa rājā sarvalokeṣu pūjyamānaḥ samantataḥ kṣudhārtaśca tathā khinno yamamāha suduḥ khitaḥ  LiP kṣuttṛṭ ca vartate deva svargatasyāpi me sadā mayā pāpaṃ kṛtaṃ kiṃ vā kiṃ kariṣyāmi vai yama  LiP yama uvācatvayā hi sumahatpāpaṃ kṛtamajñānamohataḥ harimitraṃ prati tadā vāsudevaparāyaṇam  LiP harimitre kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vāsudevārcanādiṣu tena pāpena saṃprāptaḥ kṣudrogastvāṃ sadā nṛpa  LiP dānayajñādikaṃ sarvaṃ pranaṣṭaṃ te narādhipa gītavādyasamopetaṃ gāyamānaṃ mahāmatim  LiP harimitraṃ samāhūya hṛtavānasi taddhanam upahārādikaṃ sarvaṃ vāsudevasya sannidhau  LiP tava bhṛtyaistadā luptaṃ pāpaṃ cakrustvadājñayā hareḥ kīrtiṃ vinā cānyadbrahmaṇena nṛpottama  LiP na geyayoge gātavyaṃ tasmātpāpaṃ kṛtaṃ tvayā naṣṭaste sarvalokodya gacca parvatakoṭaram  LiP pūrvotsṛṣṭaṃ svadehaṃ taṃ khādannityaṃ nikṛtya vai tasminkoṇe tvimaṃ dehaṃ khādannityaṃ kṣudhanvitaḥ  LiP mahānirayasaṃsthastvaṃ yāvanmanvantaraṃ bhavet manvantare tato tīte bhūmyāṃ tvaṃ ca bhaviṣyasi  LiP tataḥ kālena saṃprāpya mānuṣyamavagacchasi gānabandhuruvācaevamuktvā yamo vidvāṃstatraivāntaradhīyata  LiP harimitro vimānena stūyamāno gaṇādhipaiḥ viṣṇulokaṃ gataḥ śrīmān saṃgṛhya gamabāndhavān  LiP bhuvaneśo nṛpo hyasmin koṭare parvatasya vai khādamānaḥ śavaṃ nityam āste kṣuttṛṭsamanvitaḥ  LiP adrākṣaṃ taṃ nṛpaṃ tatra sarvametanmamoktavān samālokyāhamājñāya harimitraṃ sameyivān  LiP vimānenārkavarṇena gacchantamamarairvṛtam indradyumnaprasādena prāptaṃ me hyāyuruttamam  LiP tenāhaṃ harimitraṃ vai dṛṣṭavān asmi suvrata tadaiśvaryaprabhāvena mano me samupāgatam  LiP gānavidyāṃ prati tadā kinnaraiḥ samupāviśam ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇāṃ gānayogena me mune  LiP jihvā prasāditā spaṣṭā tato gānamaśikṣayam tatastu dviguṇenaiva kālenābhūdiyaṃ mama  LiP gānayogasamāyuktā gatā manvantarā daśa gānācāryo bhavaṃ tatra gandharvādyāḥ samāgatāḥ  LiP ete kinnarasaṃghā vai māmācāryamupāgatāḥ tapasā naiva śakyā vai gānavidyā tapodhana  LiP tasmācchrutena saṃyukto mattastvaṃ gānamāpnuhi evamukto munistaṃ vai praṇipatya jagau tadā  LiP tacchṛṇuṣva muniśreṣṭha vāsudevaṃ namasya tu mārkaṇḍeya uvācaulūkenaivamuktastu nārado munisattamaḥ  LiP śikṣākrameṇa saṃyuktastatra gānamāśikṣayat gānabandhustadāhedaṃ tyaktalajjo bhavādhunā  LiP ulūka uvācastrīsaṃgame tathā gīte dyūte vyākhyānasaṃgame vyavahāre tathāhāre tvarthānāṃ ca samāgame  LiP āye vyaye tathā nityaṃ tyaktalajjastu vai bhavet na kuñcitena gūḍhena nityaṃ prāvaramādibhiḥ  LiP hastavikṣepabhāvena vyādi tāsyena caiva hi niryātajihvāyogena na geyaṃ hi kathañcana  LiP na gāyedūrdhvabāhuśca nordhvadṛṣṭiḥ kathañcana svāṅgaṃ nirīkṣamāṇena paraṃ saṃprekṣatā tathā  LiP saṃghaṭṭe ca tathotthāne kaṭisthānaṃ na śasyate hāso roṣastathā kaṃpastathānyatra smṛtiḥ punaḥ  LiP naitāni śastarūpāṇi gānayoge mahāmate naikahastena śakyaṃ syāttālasaṃghaṭṭanaṃ mune  LiP kṣudhārttena bhayārtena tṛṣṇārtena tathaiva ca gānayoge na kartavyo nāndhakāre kathañcana  LiP evamādīni cānyāni na kartavyāni gāyatā mārkaṇḍeya uvācaevamuktaḥ sa bhagavāṃstenoktairvidhilakṣaṇaiḥ aśikṣayattathā gītaṃ divyaṃ varṣasahasrakam  LiP tataḥ samastasaṃpanno gītaprastārakādiṣu vipañcyādiṣu saṃpannaḥ sarvasvaravibhāgavit  LiP ayutāni ca ṣaṭtriṃśatsahasrāṇi śatāni ca svarāṇāṃ bhedayogena jñātavānmunisattamaḥ  LiP tato gandharvasaṃghāśca kinnarāṇāṃ tathaiva ca muninā saha saṃyuktāḥ prītiyuktā bhavanti te  LiP gānabandhuṃ muniḥ prāha prāpya gānamanuttamam tvāṃ samāsādya saṃpannastvaṃ hi gītaviśāradaḥ  LiP dhvāṅkṣaśatro mahāprājña kimācārya karomi te gānabandhuruvācabrahmaṇo divase brahman manavastu caturdaśa  LiP tatastrai lokyasaṃplāvo bhaviṣyati mahāmune tāvanme tvāyuṣo bhāvastāvanme paramaṃ śubham  LiP manasādhyāhitaṃ me syāddakṣiṇā munisattama nārada uvācaatītakalpasaṃyoge garuḍastvaṃ bhaviṣyasi  LiP svasti te stu mahāprājña gamiṣyāmi prasīda mām mārkaṇḍeya uvācaevamuktvā jagāmatha nāradopi janārdanam  LiP śvetadvīpe hṛṣīkeśaṃ gāpayāmāsa gītakān tatra śrutvā tu bhagavānnāradaṃ prāha mādhavaḥ  LiP tuṃbarorna viśiṣṭosi gītairadyāpi nārada yadā viśiṣṭo bhavitā taṃ kālaṃ pravadāmyaham  LiP gānabandhuṃ samāsādya gānārthajño bhavānasi manorvaivasvatasyāhamaṣṭaviśatime yuge  LiP dvāṃparāṃ te bhavaṣyāmi yudavaṃśakulodbhavaḥ devakyāṃ vasudevasya kṛṣṇo nāmnā mahāmate  LiP tadānīṃ māṃ samāsādya smārayethā yathātatham tatra tvāṃ gītasaṃpannaṃ kariṣyāmi mahāvratam  LiP tuṃbarośca samañcaiva tathātiśayasaṃyutam tāvatkālaṃ yatāyogaṃ devagandharvayoniṣu  LiP śikṣayasva yatānyāyamityuktvāntaradhīyata tato muniḥ praṇamyainaṃ tathātiśayasaṃyutam  LiP devarṣirdevasaṃkāśaḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ tapasāṃ nidhiratyantaṃ vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ  LiP skandhe vipañcīmāsādya sarvalokāṃścacāra saḥ vāruṇaṃ yāmyamāgneyamaidraṃ kauberameva ca  LiP vāyavyaṃ ca tatheśānaṃ saṃsadaṃ prāpya dharmavit gāyamāno hariṃ samyagvīṇāvādavicakṣaṇaḥ  LiP gandharvāpsarasāṃ saṃghaiḥ pūjyamānastata stataḥ brahmalokaṃ samāsādya kasmiṃścitkālaparyaye  LiP hāhāhūhūśca gandharvau gītavādyaviśāradau brahmaṇo gāyakau divyau nityau gandharvasattamau  LiP tatra tābhyāṃ samāsādya gāyamāno hariṃ prabhum brahmaṇā ca mahātejāḥ pūjito munisattamaḥ  LiP taṃ praṇamya mahātmānaṃ sarvalokapitāmaham cacāra ca yathākāmaṃ sarvalokeṣu nāradaḥ  LiP tataḥ kālena mahatā gṛhaṃ prāpya ca tuṃbaroḥ vīṇāmādāya tatrastho hyagāyata mahāmuniḥ  LiP svarakalpāstu tatrasthāḥ ṣaḍjādyāḥ sapta vai matāḥ krīḍato bhagavāndṛṣṭvā nirgataśca susatvaram  LiP śikṣayā māsa bahuśastatra tatra mahāmatiḥ śramayogena saṃyukto nāradopi mahāmuniḥ  LiP saptasvarāṅganāḥ paśyan gānavidyāviśāradaḥ āsīdvīṇā samāyoge na tāstantryaḥ prapedire  LiP tato ravaitake kṛṣṇaṃ praṇipatya mahāmuniḥ vijñāpayadaśeṣaṃ tu śvetadvīpe tu yat purā  LiP nārāyaṇena kathitaṃ gānayogamanuttamam tacchrutvā prāhasankṛṣṇaḥ prāha jāṃbavatīṃ mudā  LiP etaṃ munivaraṃ bhadre śikṣayasva yathāvidhi vīṇāgāna samāyoge tathetyuktvā ca sā harim  LiP prahasaṃtī yathāyogaṃ śikṣayāmāsa taṃ munim tataḥ saṃvatsare pūrṇe punarāgamya mādhavam  LiP praṇipatyāgratastasthau punarāha sa keśavaḥ satyāṃ samīpamāgaccha śikṣayasva yathāvidhi  LiP tathetyuktvā satyabhāmāṃ praṇipatyajagau muniḥ tayā sa sikṣito vidvān pūrṇe saṃvatsare punaḥ  LiP vāsudevamiyukto sau rukmiṇīsadanaṃ gataḥ aṅganābhistatastābhirdāsībhirmunisattamaḥ  LiP ukto sau gāyamānopi na svaraṃ vetsi vai mune tataḥ śrameṇa mahatā vatsaratrayasaṃyutam  LiP śikṣitosau tadā devyā rukmiṇyāpi jagau muniḥ tataḥ svarāṅganāḥ prāpyaḥ tantrīyogaṃ mahāmuneḥ  LiP āhūya kṛṣṇo bhagavān svayameva mahāmunim aśikṣayadameyātmā gānayogamanuttamam  LiP tato tiśayamāpannastuṃbarormunisattamaḥ tato nanarta devarṣiḥ praṇipatya janārdanam  LiP uvāca ca hṛṣīkeśaḥ sarvajñastvaṃ mahāmune prahasya gānayogena gāyasva mama sannidhau  LiP etatte prārthitaṃ prāptaṃ mama loke tathaiva ca nityaṃ tuṃbaruṇā sārdhaṃ gāyasva ca yathātatham  LiP evamukto munistatra yathāyogaṃ cacāra saḥ yadā saṃpūjayan kṛṣṇo rudraṃ bhuvananāyakam  LiP tadā jagai harestasya niyogācchaṅkarāya vai rukmiṇyā saha satyā ca jāṃbavatyā mahāmuniḥ  LiP kṛṣṇena ca nṛpaśreṣṭha śrutijātiviśāradaḥ eṣa vo muniśārdūlāḥ prokto gītakramo muneḥ  LiP brāhmaṇo vāsudevākhyāṃ gāyamāno bhṛśaṃ nṛpa hareḥ sālokyamāpnoti rudragāno dhiko bhavet  LiP anyathā narakaṃ gacchedgāyamānonyadeva hi karmaṇā manasā vācā vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ  LiP gāyan śṛṇvaṃstamāpnoti tasmādgeyaṃ paraṃ viduḥ  LiP iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge vaiṣṇavagītakathanaṃ nāma tṛtīyo dhyāyaḥṛṣaya ūcuḥvaiṣṇavā iti ye proktā vāsudevaparāyaṇāḥ kāni cihnāni teṣāṃ vai tanno brahi mahāmate  LiP teṣāṃ vā kiṃ karotyeṣa bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ etanme sarvamācakṣva sūta sarvārthavittama  LiP sūta uvācaaṃbarīṣeṇa vai pṛṣṭo mārkaṇḍeyaḥ purāmuniḥ yuṣmabhiradya yat proktaṃ tadvadāmi yathātatham  LiP mārkaṇḍeya uvācaśṛṇu rājanyathānyāyaṃ yanmāṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi yatrāste viṣṇubhaktastu tatra nārāyaṇaḥ sthitaḥ  LiP viṣṇureva hi sarvatra yeṣāṃ vai devatā smṛtā kīrtyamāne harau nityaṃ romāñco yasya vartate  LiP kaṃpaḥ svedastathakṣeṣu dṛsyante jalabindavaḥ viṣṇubhaktisamāyuktān śrautasmārtapravartakān  LiP prīto bhavati yo dṛṣṭvā vaiṣṇavo sau prakīrtitaḥ nānyadācchādayedvastraṃ vaiṣṇavo jagato raṇe  LiP viṣṇubhaktamathāyāntaṃ yo dṛṣṭvā sanmukhasthitaḥ praṇāmādi karotyevaṃ vāsudeve yathā tathā  LiP sa vai bhakta iti jñeyaḥ sa jayī syājjagattraye rūkṣākṣarāṇi śṛṇvanvai tathā bhāgavateritaḥ  LiP praṇāmapūrvaṃ kṣāntyā vai yo vadedvaiṣṇavo hi saḥ gandhapuṣpādi kaṃ sarvaṃ śirasā yo hi dhārayet  LiP hareḥ sarvamitītyevaṃ mattvāsau vaiṣṇavaḥ smṛtaḥ viṣṇukṣetre śubhānyeva karoti snehasaṃyutaḥ  LiP pratimāṃ ca harernityaṃ pūjayetprayatātmavān viṣṇubhaktaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ karmaṇā manasā girā  LiP nārāyaṇaparo nityaṃ mahābhāgavato hi saḥ bhojanārādhanaṃ sarvaṃ yathāśaktyā karoti yaḥ  LiP viṣṇubhaktasya ca sadā yathānyāyaṃ hi kathyate nārāyaṇaparo vidvānyasyānnaṃ prītamānasaḥ  LiP aśrāti taddharerāsyaṃ gatamannaṃ na saṃśayaḥ svārcanādapi viśvātmā prīto bhavati mādhavaḥ  LiP mahābhāgavate tacca dṛṣṭvāsau bhaktavatsalaḥ vāsudevaparaṃ dṛṣṭvā vaiṣṇavaṃ dagdhakilbiṣam  LiP devāpi bhītāstaṃ yānti praṇipatya yathāgatam śrūyatāṃ hi purāvṛttaṃ viṣṇubhaktasya vaibhavam  LiP dṛṣṭvā yamo pi vai bhaktaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ dagdhakilbiṣam utthāya prāñjalirbhūtvā nanāma bhṛgunandanam  LiP tasmātsaṃpūjayedbhaktyā vaiṣṇavānviṣṇuvannaraḥ sa yāti viṣṇusāmīpya nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  LiP anyabhaktasahasrebhyo viṣṇubhakto viśiṣyate viṣṇubhaktasahasrebhyo rudrabhakto viśiṣyate rudrabhaktātparataro nāstiloke na saśaṃyaḥ  LiP tasmāttu vaiṣṇavaṃ cāpi rudrabhaktamathāpi vā pūjayetsarvayatnena dharmakāmārthamuktaye  LiP iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge viṣṇubhaktakathanaṃ nāma caturtho dhyāyaḥṛṣaya ūcuḥaikṣvākuraṃbarīṣo vai vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ pālayāmāsa pṛthivīṃ sattama  LiP māhātmyamanubhāvaṃ ca bhaktiyogamanuttamam yathāvacchrotumicchāmaḥ sūta vaktuṃ tvamarhasi  LiP sūta uvācaśrūyatāṃ muniśārdūlāścaritaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ aṃbarīṣasya māhātmyaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ param  LiP triśaṅkordayitā bhāryā sarvalakṣaṇaśobhitā aṃbarīṣasya jananī nityaṃ śaucasamanvitā  LiP yoganidrāsamārūḍhaṃ śeṣaparyaṅkaśāyinam nārāyaṇaṃ mahātmānaṃ brahmāṇḍakamalodbhavam  LiP tamasā dhūpadravyādikaṃ tathā bhūmerālepanādīni haviṣāṃ pacanaṃ tathā  LiP tatkautukasamāviṣṭā svayameva cakāra sā śubhā padmāvatī nityaṃ vācā nārāyaṇeti vai  LiP anantetyeva sā nityaṃ bhāṣamāṇā pativratā dvādaśīṃ samupoṣya vai  LiP hareragre mahābhāgā suṣvāpa patinā saha tatra nārāyaṇo devastāmāha puruṣottamaḥ  LiP kim icchasi varaṃ bhadre mattas tvam brūhi bhāmini sā dṛṣṭvā tu varaṃ vavre putro me vaiṣṇavo bhavet  LiP sārvabhaumo mahātejāḥ svakarmanirataḥ śuciḥ tathetyuktvā dadau tasyai phalam ekaṃ janārdanaḥ  LiP sā prabuddhā phalaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhartre sarvaṃ nyavedayat bhakṣayāmāsa saṃhṛṣṭā phalaṃ LiP aṃbarīṣa iti khyāto loke samabhavatprabhuḥ pitaryuparate śrīmānabhiṣikto mahāmuniḥ  LiP mantriṣvādhāya rājyaṃ ca tapa ugrañcakāra saḥ saṃvatsarasahasraṃ vai japannārāyaṇaṃ prabhum  LiP hṛtpuṇḍarīkamadhyasthaṃ sūryamaṇḍalamadhyataḥ śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadhārayantaṃ caturbhujam  LiP śuddhajāṃbūnadanibhaṃ brahmaviṣṇuśivātmakam sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ pītāṃbaradharaṃ prabhum  LiP śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ devaṃ puruṣaṃ puruṣottamam tato garuḍamāruhya sarvadevairabhiṣṭutaḥ  LiP ājagāma sa viśvātmā sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥ airāvatamivācintyaṃ kṛtvā vai garuḍaṃhariḥ  LiP svayaṃ śakra kavyavāhaḥ kapālī tvaṃ havyavāhaḥ prabhañjanaḥ  LiP ādidevaḥ kriyānandaḥ paramātmātmanī sthitaḥ tvāṃ prapannosmigovinda jaya devakinandana jaya deva jagannātha pāhi māṃ puṣkarekṣaṇa  LiP nānyā aṃbarīṣa uvācalokanātha parānanda nityaṃ me vartate matiḥ vāsudevaparo nityaṃ vāṅmanaḥ kāyakarmabhiḥ  LiP yathā tvaṃ devadevasya bhavasya paramātmanaḥ tathā bhavāmyahaṃ viṣṇo tava deva janārdana  LiP pāliyiṣyāmi pṛthivīṃ kṛtvā vai vaiṣṇavaṃ jagat yajñahomārcanaiścaiva tarpayāmi surottamān  LiP vaiṣṇavānpālayiṣyāmi nihaniṣyāmi śātravān lokatāpabhaye bhīta iti me dhīyate matiḥ  LiP śrībhagavānuvācaevamastu yathecchaṃ vai cakrametatsudarśanam purā rudraprasādena labdhaṃ vai durlabhaṃ mayā  LiP ṛṣiśāpādikaṃ duḥkhaṃ śatrurogādikaṃ tathā nihaniṣyati te nityamityuktvāntaradhīyata  LiP sūta uvācatataḥ praṇamya mudito rājā nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum praviśya nagarīṃ ramyāmayodhyāṃ paryapālayat  LiP brāhmaṇādīṃśca varṇāṃśca svasvakarmaṇy ayojayat nārāyaṇaparo nityaṃ viṣṇubhaktānakalmaṣān  LiP pālayāmāsa hṛṣṭātmā viśeṣeṇa janādhipaḥ aśvamedhaśatairiṣṭvā vājapeyaśatena ca  LiP pālayāmāsa pṛthivīṃ sāgarāvaraṇāmimām gṛhegṛhe haristasthau vedaghoṣo gṛhegṛhe  LiP nāmaghoṣo hareścaiva yajñaghoṣastathaiva ca abhavannṛpaśārdūle tasmin rājyaṃ praśāsati  LiP nāsasyā nātṛṇā bhūmirna durbhikṣādibhiryutā rāgahīnāḥ prajā nityaṃ sarvopadravavarjitāḥ  LiP aṃbarīṣo mahātejāḥ pālayāmāsa medinīm tasyaivaṃvartamānasya kanyā kamalalocanā  LiP śrīmatī nāma vikhyātā sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutā pradānasamayaṃ prāptā devamāyeva śobhanā  LiP tasminkāle muniḥ śrīmānnārado bhyāgataścavai aṃbarīṣasya rājño vai parvataśca mahāmatiḥ  LiP tāvubhāvāgatau dṛṣṭvā praṇipatya yathāvidhi aṃbarīṣo mahātejāḥ pūjayāmāsa tāv ṛṣī  LiP kanyāṃ tāṃ ramamāṇāṃ vai meghamadhye śatahradām prāha tāṃ prekṣya bhagavān nāradaḥ sasmitas tadā  LiP keyaṃ rājanmahābhāgā kanyā surasutopamā brūhi dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha sarvalakṣaṇaśobhitā  LiP rājovācaduhiteyaṃ mama vibho śrīmatī nāma nāmataḥ pradānasamayaṃ prāptā varamanveṣate śubhā  LiP ityukto muniśārdūlastāmaicchannārado dvijāḥ parvatopi munistāṃ vai cakame munisattamāḥ  LiP anujñāpya ca rājānaṃ nārado vākyamabravīt rahasyāhūya dharmātmāmama dehi sutāmimām  LiP parvato hi tathā prāha rājānaṃ rahasi prabhuḥ tāvubhau saha dharmātmā praṇipatya bhayārditaḥ  LiP ubhau bhavantau kanyāṃ me pārthayānau kathaṃ tvaham kariṣyāmi mahāprājña śṛṇu nārada me vacaḥ  LiP tvaṃ ca parvata me vākyaṃ śṛṇu vakṣyāmi yatprabho kanyeyaṃ yuvayorekaṃ varayiṣyati cecchubhā  LiP tasmai kanyāṃ prayacchāmi nānyathā śaktirasti me tathetyuktvā tato bhūyaḥ śvo yāsyāva iti sma ha  LiP ityuktvā munisārdūlau jagmatuḥ prītimānasau vāsudevaparau nityamubhau jñānavidāṃvarau  LiP viṣṇu lokaṃ tato gatvā nārado munisattamaḥ praṇipatya hṛṣīkeśaṃ vākyametaduvāca ha  LiP śrotavyamasti bhagavannātha nārāyaṇa prabho rahasi tvāṃ pravakṣyāmi namaste bhuvaneśvara  LiP tataḥ prahasya govindaḥ sarvānutsārya taṃ munim brūhītyāha ca viśvātmā munirāha ca keśavam  LiP tvadīyo nṛpatiḥ śrīmānaṃbarīṣo mahīpatiḥ tasya kanyā viśālākṣī śrīmatī nāma nāmataḥ  LiP pariṇetumanāstatra gato smi vacanaṃ śṛṇu parvato yaṃ muniḥ śrīmāṃstava bhṛtyastaponidhiḥ  LiP tāmaicchatsopi bhagavannāvāmāha janādhipaḥ aṃbarīṣo mahātejāḥ kanyeyaṃ yuvayorvaram  LiP lāvaṇyayuktaṃ vṛṇuyādyadi tasmai dadāmyaham ityāhāvāṃ nṛpastatra tathetyuktvāhamāgataḥ  LiP āgamiṣyāmi te rājan śvaḥ prabhāte gṛhaṃ tviti āgatohaṃ jagannātha kartumarhasi me priyam  LiP vānarānanavadbhāti parvatasya mukhaṃ yathā tathā kuru jagannātha mama cedicchasi priyam  LiP tathetyuktvā sa govindaḥ prahasta madhusūdanaḥ tvayoktaṃ ca kariṣyāmi gaccha saumya yathāgatam  LiP evamuktvā munirhṛṣṭaḥ praṇipatya janārdanam manyamānaḥ kṛtātmānaṃ tathāyodhyāṃ jagāma saḥ  LiP gate munivare tasminparvato pi mahāmuniḥ praṇamya mādhavaṃ hṛṣṭo rahasyenamuvāca ha  LiP vṛttaṃ tasya nivedyāgre nāradasya jagatpateḥ golāṅgūlamukhaṃ yadvanmukhaṃ bhāti tathā kuru  LiP tacchrutvā bhagavānviṣṇustvayoktaṃ ca karomi vai gaccha śīghramayodhyāṃ vai māvedīrnāradasya vai  LiP tvayā me saṃvidaṃ tatra tathetyuktvā jagāma saḥ tato rājā samājñāya prāptau munivarau tadā  LiP māṅgalyairvividhaiḥ sarvāmayodhyāṃ dhvajamālinīm maḍaṃyāmāsa puṣpaiśca lājairścaiva samantataḥ  LiP aṃbusiktagṛhadvārāṃ siktāpaṇamahāpathām divyagandharasopetāṃ dhūpitāṃ divyadhūpakaiḥ  LiP kṛtvā ca nagarīṃ rājā maṇḍayāmāsa tāṃ sabhām divyairgandhaistathā dhūpai ratnaiśca vividhaistathā  LiP alaṅkṛtāṃ maṇistaṃbhairnānāmālyopaśobhitām parārdhyāstaraṇopetairdivyairbhadrāsanairvṛtām  LiP kṛtvā nṛpendrastāṃ kanyāṃ hyādāya praviveśa ha sarvābharaṇasaṃpannāṃ śrīrivāyatalojanām  LiP karasaṃmitamadhyāṅgīṃ pañcasnigdhāṃ śubhānanām strībhiḥ parivṛtāṃ divyāṃ śrīmatīṃ saṃśritāṃ tadā  LiP sabhā ca sā bhūpapeḥ samṛddhā maṇipravekottamaratnacitrā nyastā sanā mālyavatī subaddhā tāmāyayuste nararājavargāḥ  LiP athāparo brahmavarātmajo hi traividyavidyo bhagavānmahātmā saparvato brahmavidāṃva riṣṭho mahāmunirnārada ājagāma  LiP tāvagatau samīkṣyātha rājā saṃbhrāntamānasaḥ divyamāsanāmādāya pūjayāmāsa tāvubhau  LiP ubhau devarṣisiddhau tau ubhau jñānavidāṃ varau samāsīnau mahātmānau kanyārthaṃ munisattamau  LiP tāvubhau praṇipatyāgre kanyāṃ tāṃ śrīmatīṃ śubhām sutāṃ kamalapatrākṣīṃ prāha rājā yaśasvinīm  LiP anayoryaṃ varaṃ bhadre manasā tmavihecchasi tasmai mālāmimāndehi praṇipatya yathāvidhi  LiP evamuktā tu sā kanyā strībhiḥ parivṛtā tadā mālāṃ hiraṇmayīṃ divyāmādāya subhalocanā  LiP yatrāsīnau mahātmānau tatrāgamyasthitā tadā vīkṣamāṇā muniśreṣṭhau nāradaṃ parvataṃ tathā  LiP muniśreṣṭhaṃ na paśyāmi nāradaṃ parvataṃ tathā anayormadhyatastvekamūnaṣoḍaśavārṣikam  LiP saṃbhrāntamānasā tatra pravātakadalī yathā tasthau tāmahā rājāsau vatse kiṃ tvaṃ kariṣyasi  LiP anayoreka muddiśya dehi mālāmimāṃ śubhe sā prāha pitaraṃ trastā imau tau naravānarau  LiP muniśreṣṭhaṃ na paśyāmi nāradaṃ parvataṃ tathā anayormadhyatastvekamūnaṣoḍaśavārṣikam  LiP sarvābharaṇasaṃpannamatasīpuṣpasaṃnibham dīrghabāhuṃ viśālākṣaṃ tuṅgīrasthalam uttamam  LiP rekhāṅkitakaṭigrīvaṃ raktāntāyatalocanam namracāpānukaraṇapaṭubhrūyugaśobhitam  LiP vibhaktatrivalīvyaktaṃ nābhivyaktaśubhodaram hiraṇyāṃbarasaṃvītaṃ tuṅgaratnanakhaṃ śubham padmākārakaraṃ tvenaṃ padmāsyaṃ padmalocanam  LiP sunāsaṃ padmahṛdayaṃ padmanābhaṃ śriyā vṛtam dantapaṅktibhiratyarthaṃ kundakuḍmalasannibhaiḥ  LiP hasaṃtaṃ māṃ samālokya dakṣiṇaṃ ca prasārya vai pāṇiṃ sthitamamuṃ tatra paśyāmi śubhamūrdhajam  LiP saṃbhrāntamānasāṃ tatra vepatīṃ kadalīmiva sthitāṃ tāmāha rājāsau vatse kiṃ tvaṃ kariṣyasi  LiP evamukte muniḥ prāha nāradaḥ saṃśayaṅgataḥ kiyanto bāhavastasya kanye brūhi yathātatham  LiP bāhudvayaṃ ca paśyāmītyāha kanyā śucismitā prāha tāṃ parvatastatra tasya vakṣaḥsthale śubhe  LiP kiṃ paśyasi ca me brūhi kare kiṃ vāsya paśyasi kanyā tamāha mālāṃ vai pañcarūpāmanuttamām  LiP vakṣaḥsthale sya paśyāmi kare kārmukasāyakān evamuktau muniśreṣṭhau parasparamanuttamau  LiP manasā cintayantau tau māyeyaṃ kasyacid bhavet māyāvī taskaro nūnaṃ svayameva janārdanaḥ  LiP āgato na yatā kuryātkathamasmanmukhaṃ tvidam golāṅgūlatvamityevaṃ cintayā māsa nāradaḥ  LiP parvatopi yathānyāyaṃ vānaratvaṃ kathaṃ mama prāptamityeva manasā cintāmāpedivāṃstathā  LiP tato rājā praṇamyāsau nāradaṃ parvataṃ tathā bhavadbhyāṃ kimidaṃ tatra kṛtaṃ buddhivimohajam  LiP svasthau bhavantau tiṣṭhetāṃ yathā kanyārtha mudyatau evamuktau muniśreṣṭhau nṛpamūcaturulbaṇau  LiP tvameva mohaṃ kuruṣe nāvāmiha kathañcana āvayorekameṣā te varayatveva māciram  LiP tataḥ sā kanyakā bhūyaḥ praṇiptayeṣṭadevatām māyāmādāya tiṣṭhantaṃ tayormadhye samāhitam  LiP sarvābharaṇasaṃyukta matasīpuṣpasannibham dīrghabāhuṃ supuṣṭāṅgaṃ karṇāntāyatalocanam  LiP pūrvavatpuruṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā mālāṃ tasmai dadau hi sā anantaraṃ hi sā kanyā na dṛṣṭā manujaiḥ punaḥ  LiP tato nādaḥ samabhavat kimetaditi vismitau tāmādāya gato viṣṇuḥ svasthānaṃ puruṣottamaḥ  LiP purā tadarthamaniśaṃ tapastaptvā varāṅganā śrīmatī sā samutpannā sā gatā ca tathā harim  LiP tāvubhau muniśārdūlau dhikkṛtāvati duḥkhitau vāsudevaṃ prati tadā jagmaturbhavanaṃ hareḥ  LiP tāvāgatau samīkṣyāha śrīmatiṃ bhagavānhariḥ muniśreṣṭhau samāyātau gūhasvātmānamatra vai  LiP tathetyuktvā ca sā devī prahasaṃtī cakāra ha nāradaḥ praṇipatyāgre prāha dāmodaraṃ harim  LiP priyaṃ hi kṛtavānadya mama tvaṃ parvatasya hi tvameva nūnaṃ govinda kanyāṃ tāṃ hṛtavānāsi  LiP vimohyāvāṃ svayaṃ buddhyā pratārya surasattama ityuktaḥ puraṣo viṣṇuḥ pidhāya śrotramacyutaḥ pāṇibhyāṃ prāha bhagavān bhavadbhyāṃ kimudīritam  LiP kāmavānapi bhāvoyaṃ munivṛttiraho kila evamukto muniḥ prāha vāsudevaṃ sa nāradaḥ  LiP karṇamūle mama kathaṃ golāṅgūlamukhaṃ tviti karṇamūle tamāhedaṃ vānaratvaṃ kṛtaṃ mayā  LiP parvatasya mayā vidvan golāṅgūlamukhaṃ tava mayā tava kṛtaṃ tatra priyārthaṃ nānyathā tviti  LiP parvato pi tathā prāha tasyāpyevaṃ jagādasaḥ śṛṇvatorubhayostatra prāha dāmodaro vacaḥ  LiP priyaṃ bhavadbhyāṃ kṛtavān satyenātmānamālabhe nāradaḥ prāha dharmātmā āvayormadhyataḥ sthitaḥ  LiP dhanuṣmān puruṣaḥ ko ḥtra tāṃ hṛtvā gatavānkila tac chrutvā vāsudevo sau prāha tau munisattamau  LiP māyāvino mahātmano bahavaḥ saṃti sattamāḥ tatra sā śrīmatī nūnamadṛṣṭvā munisattamau  LiP cakrapāṇirahaṃ nityaṃ caturbāhuriti sthitaḥ tāṃ tathā nāhamaicchaṃ vai bhavadbhyāṃ viditaṃ hi tat  LiP ityuktau praṇipatyainamūcatuḥ prītimānasau ko tra doṣastava vibho nārāyaṇa jagatpate  LiP daurātmyaṃ tannṛpasyaiva māyāṃ hi kṛtavānasau ityuktvā jagmatustasmānmunīnāradaparvatau  LiP aṃbarīṣaṃ samāsādya śāpenainamayojayat nāradaḥ parvataścaiva yasmādāvāmihāgatau  LiP āhūya paścādanyasmai kanyāṃ tvaṃ dattavānasi māyāyogena tasmāttvaṃ tamo hyabhibhaviṣyati  LiP tena cātmānamatyarthaṃ yathāvattvaṃ ca vetsyasi evaṃ śāpepradatte tu tamorāśirathotthitaḥ  LiP nṛpaṃ prati tataścakraṃ viṣṇoḥ prādurabhūt kṣaṇāt cakravitrāsitaṃ ghoraṃ tāvubhau tama abhyagāt  LiP tataḥ saṃtrastasarvāṅgau dhāvamānau mahāmunī pṛṣṭhataścakramālokya tamorāśiṃ durāsadam  LiP kanyāsiddhiraho prāptā hyāvayoriti vegitau lokālokāntamaniśaṃ dhāvamānau bhayārditau  LiP trāhitrāhīti govindaṃ bhāṣamāṇau bhayārditau viṣṇulokaṃ tato gatvā nārāyaṇa jagatpate  LiP vāsudeva hṛṣīkeśa padmanābha janārdana trāhyāvāṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa nātho si puruṣottama  LiP tato nārāyaṇaścintya śrīmāñchrīvatsalāñchanaḥ nivārya cakraṃ dhvāntaṃ ca bhaktānugrahakāmyayā  LiP aṃbarīṣaśca madbhaktastathaitau munisattamau anayorasya ca tathā hitaṃ kāryaṃ mayādhunā  LiP āhūya tattamaḥ śrīmān girā prahlādayan hariḥ provāca bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śṛṇutāṃ ma idaṃvacaḥ  LiP ṛṣiśāpo na caivāsīdanyathā ca varo mama datto nṛpāya rakṣārthaṃ nāsti tasyānyathā punaḥ  LiP aṃbarīṣasya putrasyanaptuḥ putro mahāyaśāḥ śrīmāndasaratho nāma rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ  LiP tasyāhamagrajaḥ putro rāmanāmā bhavāmyaham tatra me dakṣiṇobāhurbharato nāma vai bhavet  LiP śatrughno nāma savyaśca śeṣo sau lakṣmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ tatra māṃ samupāgaccha gacchedānīṃ nṛpaṃ vinā  LiP muniśreṣṭhau ca hitvā tvamiti smāha ca mādhavaḥ evam uktaṃ tamo nāśaṃ tatkṣaṇāc ca jagāma vai  LiP nivāritaṃ hareścakraṃ yathāpūrvamatiṣṭhata muniśreṣṭhau bhayānmuktau praṇipatya janārdanam  LiP nirgatau śokasaṃtaptau ūcatustau parasparam adyaprabhṛti dehāntamāvāṃ kanyāparigraham  LiP na kariṣyāva ityuktvā pratijñāya ca tāvṛṣī yogadhyānaparau śuddhau yathāpūrvaṃ vyavasthitau  LiP aṃbarīṣaśca rājāsau paripālya ca medinīm sabhṛtyajñātisaṃpanno viṣṇulokaṃ jagāma vai  LiP mānārthamaṃbarīṣasya tathaiva munisiṃhayoḥ rāmo dāśarathir bhūtvā nātmavedīśvaro bhavat  LiP munayaśca tathā sarve bhṛgvādyā munisattamāḥ māyā na kāryā vidvadbhirityāhuḥ prekṣyataṃ harim  LiP nāradaḥ parvataścaiva ciraṃ jñātvā viceṣṭitam māyāṃ viṣṇorvinindyaiva rudrabhaktau babhūvatuḥ  LiP etaddhi kathitaṃsarva mayā yuṣmākamadya vai aṃbarīṣasya māhātmyaṃ māyāvitvaṃ ca vai hareḥ  LiP yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvāpi mānavaḥ māyāṃ visṛjya puṇyātmā rudralokaṃ sa gacchati  LiP idaṃ pavitraṃ paramaṃ puṇyaṃ vedairudīritam sāyaṃ prātaḥ paṭhennityaṃ viṣṇoḥ sāyujyamāpnuyāt  LiP iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge śrīmatyākhyānaṃ nāma pañcamo dhyāyaḥṛṣaya ūcuḥmāyāvitvaṃ śrutaṃ viṣṇordevadevasya dhīmataḥ kathaṃ jyeṣṭhāsamutpattirdevadevājjanārdanāt  LiP vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ lomaharṣaṇa tattvataḥ sūta uvācaanādinidhanaḥ śrīmāndhātā nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ  LiP jagaddvaidhamidaṃ cakre mohanāya jagatpatiḥ viṣṇurvai brāhmaṇānvedānvedadharmān sanātanān  LiP śriyaṃ padmāṃ tathā śreṣṭhāṃ bhāgamekamakārayat jyeṣṭhāmalakṣmīmaśubhāṃ vedabāhyānnarādhamān  LiP adharmaṃ ca mahātejā bhāgameka makalpayat alakṣmīmagrataḥ sṛṣṭvā paścātpadmāṃ janārdanaḥ  LiP jyeṣṭhā tena samākhyātā alakṣmīrdvijasattamāḥ amṛtodbhavavelāyāṃ viṣānantaramulbaṇāt  LiP aśubhā sā tathotpannā jyeṣṭhā iti ca vai śrutam tataḥ śrīśca samutpannā padmā viṣṇuparigrahaḥ  LiP duḥsaho nāma viprarṣirupayeme śubhāṃ tadā jyeṣṭhāṃ tāṃ paripūrṇo sau manasā vīkṣya dhiṣṭhitām  LiP lokaṃ cacāraṃ hṛṣṭātmā tayā saha munistadā yasmin ghoṣo hareścaiva harasya ca mahātmanaḥ  LiP vedaghoṣastathā viprā homadhūmastathaiva ca bhasmāṅgino vā yatrāsaṃstatra tatra bhayārditā  LiP pidhāya karṇau saṃyāti dhāvamānā itastataḥ jyeṣṭhāmevaṃvidhāṃ dṛṣṭvā duḥsaho mohamāgataḥ  LiP tayā saha vanaṃ gatvā cacāra sa mahāmuniḥ tapo mahadvane ghore yāti kanyā pratigraham  LiP na kariṣyāmi cetyuktvā pratijñāya ca tāmṛṣiḥ yogajñānaparaḥ śuddho yatra yogīśvaro muniḥ  LiP tatrāyāntaṃ mahātmānaṃ mārkaṇḍeyamapaśyata praṇipatya mahātmānaṃ duḥsaho munimabravīt  LiP bhāryeyaṃ bhagavanmahyaṃ na sthāsyati kathañcana kiṃ karomīti viprarṣe hyanayā saha bhāryayā  LiP praviśāmi tathā kutra kuto na praviśāmyaham mārkaṇḍeya uvācaśṛṇu duḥsaha sarvatra akīrtiraśubhānvitā  LiP alakṣmīratulā ceyaṃ jyeṣṭhā ityabhiśabditā nārāyaṇaparā yatra vedamārgānusāriṇaḥ  LiP rudrabhaktā mahātmāno bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ sthitā yatra janā nityaṃ mā viśethāḥ kathañcana  LiP nārāyaṇa hṛṣīkeśa puṇḍarīkākṣa mādhava acyutānanta govinda vāsudeva janārdana  LiP rudra rudreti rudreti śivāya ca namo namaḥ namaḥ śivatarāyeti śaṅkarāyeti sarvadā  LiP mahādeva mahādeva mahādeveti kīrtayet umāyāḥ pataye caiva hiraṇyapataye sadā  LiP hiraṇyabāhave tubhyaṃ vṛṣāṅkāya namo namaḥ nṛsiṃhavāmanācintya mādhaveti ca ye janāḥ  LiP vakṣyanti satataṃ hṛṣṭā brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāstathā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāśca ye nityaṃ teṣāṃ dhanagṛhādiṣu ārāme caiva goṣṭheṣu na viśethāḥ kathañcana  LiP jvālāmālākarālaṃ ca sahasrādityasannibham cakraṃ viṣṇoratīvograṃ teṣāṃ hanti sadāśubham  LiP svāhākāro vaṣaṭkāro gṛhe yasmin hi vartate taddhitvā cānyamāgaccha samāghoṣetha yatra vā  LiP vedābhyāsaratā nityaṃ nityakarmaparāyaṇāḥ vāsudevārcanaratā dūratastānvisarjayet  LiP agnihotraṃ gṛhe yeṣāṃ liṅgārcā vā gṛheṣu ca vāsudevatanurvāpi caṇḍikā yatra tiṣṭhati  LiP dūrato vraja tān hitvā sarvapāpavivarjitān nityanaimittikairyajñairyajanti ca maheśvaram  LiP tān hitvā vraja cānyatra duḥsahatvaṃ sahānayā śrotriyā brāhmaṇā gāvo guravo tithayaḥ sadā  LiP rudrabhaktāśca pūjyante yairnityaṃ tānvivarjayet duḥsaha uvācayasminpraveśo yogyo me tadbrūhi munisattama  LiP tvadvākyādbhayanirmukto viśānmeṣāṃ gṛhe sadā mārkaṇḍeya uvācana śrotriyā dvijā gāvo guravo tithayaḥ sadā yatra bhartā ca bhāryā ca parasparavirodhinau  LiP sabhāryastvaṃ gṛhaṃ tasya viśethā bhayavarjitaḥ devadevo mahādevo rudrastribhuvaneśvaraḥ  LiP vinindyo yatra bhagavān viśasva bhayavarjitaḥ vāsudevaratirnāsti yatra nāsti sadāśivaḥ  LiP japahomādikaṃ nāsti bhasma nāsti gṛhe nṛṇām parvaṇyabhyarcanaṃ nāsti caturdaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ  LiP kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ ca rudrasya saṃdhyāyāṃ bhasmavarjitāḥ caturdaśyāṃ mahādevaṃ na yajanti ca yatra vai  LiP viṣṇornāmavihinā ye saṃgatāśca durātmabhiḥ namaḥ kṛṣṇāya śarvāya śivāya parameṣṭhine  LiP brāhmaṇāśca narā mūḍhā navadanti durātmakāḥ tatraiva satataṃ vatsa sabhāryastvaṃ samāvisa  LiP vedaghoṣo na yatrāsti gurupūjādayo na ca pitṛkarmavihīnāṃstu sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa  LiP rātrau rātrau gṛhe yasmin kalaho vartate mithaḥ anayā sārdhamaniśaṃ viśa tvaṃ bhayavarjitaḥ  LiP liṅgārcanaṃ yasya nāsti yasya nāsti japādikam rudrabhaktirvinindā ca tatraiva viśa nirbhayaḥ  LiP atithiḥ śrotriyo vāpi gururvāvaiṣṇavopi vā na saṃti yadgṛhe gāvaḥ sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa  LiP bālānāṃ prekṣamāṇānāṃ yatrādattvā tvabhakṣayan bhakṣyāṇi tatra saṃhṛṣṭaḥ sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa  LiP anabhyarcya mahādevaṃ vāsudevamathāpi vā ahutvā vidhivadyatra tatra nityaṃ samāviśa  LiP pāpa karmaratā mūḍhā dayāhīnāḥ parasparam gṛhe yasminsamāsaṃte deśe vā tatra saṃviśa  LiP prākārāgāravidhvaṃsā na caiveḍyā kuṭuṃbinī tadgṛhaṃ tu samāsādya vasa nityaṃ hi hṛṣṭadhīḥ  LiP yatra kaṇṭakino vṛkṣā yatra niṣpāvavallarī brahmavṛkṣaśca yatrāsti sabhāryāstvaṃ samāviśa  LiP agastyārkādayo vāpi bandhujīvo gṛheṣu vai karavīro viśeṣeṇa nandyāvartamathāpi vā  LiP mallikā vā gṛhe yeṣāṃ sabhāryāstvaṃ samāviśa kanyā ca yatra vai vallī drohī vā ca jaṭī gṛhe  LiP bahulā kadalī yatra sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa tālaṃ tamālaṃ bhallātaṃ tittiḍīkhaṇḍameva ca  LiP kadaṃbaḥ khādiraṃ vāpi sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa nyagrodhaṃ vā gṛhe yeṣāmaśvatthaṃ cūtameva vā  LiP uduṃbaraṃ vā panasaṃ sabhāryāstvaṃ samāviśa yasya kākagṛhaṃ niṃbe ārāme vā gṛhepi vā  LiP daṇḍinī muṇḍinī vāpi sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa ekā dāsī gṛhe yatra trigavaṃ pañcamāhiṣam  LiP ṣaḍaśvaṃ saptamātaṅgaṃ sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa yasya kālī gṛhe devī pretarūpā ca ḍākinī  LiP kṣetrapālethavā yatra sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa bhikṣubiṃbaṃ ca vai yasya gṛhe kṣapaṇakaṃ tathā  LiP bauddhaṃ vā biṃbamāsādya tatra pūrṇaṃ samāviśa śayanāsanakāleṣu bhojanāṭanavṛttiṣu  LiP yeṣāṃ vadati no vāṇī nāmāni ca hareḥ sadā tadgahaṃ te samākhyātaṃ sabhāryasya niveśitum  LiP pāṣaṇḍācāraniratāḥ śrautasmārtabahiṣkṛtāḥ viṣṇubhakti vinirmuktā mahādevavinindakāḥ  LiP nāstikāśca śaṭhā yatra sabhāryāstvaṃ samāviśa sarvasmādadhikatvaṃ ye na vadanti pinākinaḥ  LiP sādhāraṇaṃ smarantyenaṃ sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa brahmā ca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ śakraḥ sarvasureśvaraḥ  LiP rudraprasādajāśceti na vadanti durātmakāḥ brahmā ca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ śakraśca sama eva ca  LiP vadanti mūḍhāḥ khadyotaṃ bhānuṃ vā mūḍhacetasaḥ teṣāṃ gṛhe tathā kṣetra āvāse vā sadānayā  LiP viśa bhuṅkṣva gṛhaṃ teṣāṃ api pūrṇamananyadhīḥ ye śranti kevalaṃ mūḍhāḥ pakvamannaṃ vicetasaḥ  LiP snānamaṅgalahīnāś ca teṣāṃ tvaṃ gṛham āviśa yā nārī śaucavibhraṣṭā dehasaṃskāravarjitā  LiP sarvabhakṣaratā nityaṃ tasyāḥ stāne samāviśa malināsyāḥ svayaṃ martyā malināṃbaradhāriṇaḥ  LiP maladantā gṛhasthāśca gṛhe teṣāṃ samāviśa pādaśaucavinirmuktāḥ saṃdhyākāle ca śāyinaḥ  LiP saṃdhyāyāma śrute ye vai gṛhaṃ teṣāṃ samāviśa atyāśanaratā martyā atipānaratā narāḥ  LiP dyūtavādakriyāmūḍhāḥ gṛhe teṣāṃ samāviśa brahmasvahāriṇo ye cāyogyāṃścaiva yajanti vā  LiP śūdrānnabhojino vāpi gṛhaṃ teṣāṃ samāviśa madyapānaratāḥ pāpā māṃsa bhakṣaṇatatparāḥ  LiP paradāraratā martyā gṛhaṃ teṣāṃ samāviśa parvaṇyanarcābhiratā maithune vā divā ratāḥ  LiP saṃdhyāyāṃ maithunaṃ yeṣāṃ gṛhe teṣāṃ samāviśa pṛṣṭhato maithunaṃ yeṣāṃ śvānavanmṛgavacca vā  LiP jale vā maithunaṃ kuryātsabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa rajasvalāṃ striyaṃ gaccheccāṇḍālīṃ vā narādhamaḥ  LiP kanyāṃ vā gogṛhe vāpi gṛhaṃ teṣāṃ samāviśa bahunā kiṃ pralāpena nityakarmabahiṣkṛtāḥ  LiP rudrabhaktivihīnāye gṛhaṃ teṣāṃ samāviśa śṛṅgairdivyauṣadhaiḥ kṣudraiḥ śepha ālipya gacchati  LiP bhagadrāvaṃ karotyasmātsabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa sūta uvācaityuktvā sa muniḥ śrīmān nirmārjya nayane tadā  LiP brahmarṣirbrahmasaṃkāśastatraivāntarddhimātanot duḥsahaśca tathoktāni stānāni ca samīyivān  LiP viśeṣāddevadevasya viṣṇornidāratātmanām sabhāryo muniśārdūlaḥ saiṣā jyeṣṭhā iti smṛtā  LiP duḥsahastāmuvācedaṃ taḍāgāśramamantare āsva tvamatra cāhaṃ vai pravekṣyāmi rasātalam  LiP āvayoḥ sthānamālokya nivāsārthaṃ tataḥ punaḥ āgamiṣyāmi te pārśvamityuktā tamuvāca sā  LiP kimaśrāmi mahābhāga ko me dāsyati vai balim ityuktastāṃ muniḥ prāha yāḥ striyastvāṃ yajanti vai  LiP balibhiḥ puṣpadhūpaiśca na tāsāṃ ca gṛhaṃ viśa ityuktvā tvāviśattatra pātālaṃ bilayogataḥ  LiP adyāpi ca vinirmagno muniḥ sa jalasaṃstare grāmaparvatabāhyeṣu nityamāste śubhā punaḥ  LiP prasaṃgāddevandeveśo viṣṇustribhuvaneśvaraḥ lakṣmyā dṛṣṭastayā lakṣmīḥ sā tamāha janārdanam  LiP bhartā gato mahābāho bilaṃ tyaktvā sa māṃ prabho anāthāhaṃ jagannātha vṛttiṃ dehi namostu te  LiP sūta uvācaityukto bhagavānviṣṇuḥ prahasyāha janārdanaḥ jyeṣṭhāmalakṣmīṃ deveśo mādhavo madhusūdanaḥ  LiP śrīviṣṇuruvācaye rudramanaghaṃ śarvaṃ śaṅkaraṃ nīlalohitam aṃbāṃ haimavatīṃ vāpi janitrīṃ jagatāmapi  LiP madbhaktānnindayantyatra teṣāṃ vittaṃ tavaiva hi yepi caiva mahādevaṃ vinindyaiva yajanti mām  LiP mūḍhā hyabhāgyā madbhaktā api teṣāṃ dhanaṃ tava yasyājñayā hyahaṃ brahmā prasādādvartate sadā  LiP ye yajanti vinindyaiva mama vidveṣakārakāḥ madbhaktā naiva te bhaktā iva vartanti durmadāḥ  LiP teṣāṃ gṛhaṃ dhanaṃ kṣetramiṣṭāpūrtaṃ tavaiva hi sūta uvācaityuktvā tāṃ parityajya lakṣmyālakṣmīṃ janārdanaḥ  LiP jajāpa bhagavanrudramalakṣmīkṣayasiddhaye tasmātpradeyastasyai ca balirnityaṃmunīśvarāḥ  LiP viṣṇubhaktairna saṃdehaḥ sarvayatnena sarvadā aṅganābhiḥ sadā pūjyā balibhirvividhairdvijāḥ  LiP yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān alakṣmīvṛttamanagho lakṣmīvāllaṃbhate gatim  LiP iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge alakṣmīvṛttaṃ nāma ṣaṣṭhe dhyāyaḥṛṣaya ūcuḥkiñjapānmucyate jantuḥ sarvalokabhayādibhiḥ sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim  LiP alakṣmīṃvātha saṃtyajya gamiṣyati LiP mamātra nidhanaṃ śreyo na kathañcana jīvitam ityuktaḥ sa ca nirgamya yajñavāṭaṃ jagāma vai  LiP tasminyāte dvijānāṃ tu na mantrāḥ pratipedire aitareye sthitetatra brāhmaṇā mohitāstadā  LiP tato iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge dvādaśākṣarapraśaṃsānāma saptamo dhyāyaḥsuta uvācaaṣṭākṣaro dvijaśreṣṭhā namo nārāyaṇeti ca dvādaśākṣaramantraśca paramaḥ paramātmanaḥ  LiP mantra ṣaḍakṣaro viprāḥ prasādādrudrasya uṣṭradehamajājñayā śilādaputramāsādya namaskṛtya vidhānataḥ  LiP meruṣṭaṣṭhe munivaraḥ śrutvā dharmamanuttamam māheśvaraṃ muniśreṣṭhā hyapṛcchacca punaḥ punaḥ  LiP nandinaṃ praṇipatyainaṃ kathaṃ paśupatiḥ prabhuḥ vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ tatsarvaṃ ca tadāha saḥ  LiP tatsarvaṃ śrutavān vyāsaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ tasmādahanumaśrutya yuṣmākaṃ pravadāmi vai  LiP sarve śṛṇvaṃ tu vacanaṃ namaskṛtvā maheśvaram sanatkumāra uvācakathaṃ paśupatirdevaḥ paśavaḥ ke prakīrtitāḥ  LiP kaiḥ pāśaiste nibadhyante vimucyante ca te katham śailādir uvācasanatkumāra vakṣyāmi sarvam etad yathātatham  LiP rudrabhaktasya śāntasya tava kalyāmacetasaḥ brahmādyāḥ sthāvarāntāśca devadevasya dhīmataḥ  LiP paśavaḥ parikīrtyante saṃsāravaśavartinaḥ teṣāṃ patitvādbhagavān rudraḥ paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP anādinidhano dhātā bhagavānviṣṇuravyayaḥ māyāpāśena badhnāti paśuvatparameśvaraḥ  LiP sa eva mocakasteṣāṃ jñānayogena sevitaḥ avidyāpāśabaddhānāṃ nānyo mocaka iṣyate  LiP tamṛte paramātmānaṃ śaṅkaraṃ parameśvaram caturviṃśatitattvāni pāśā hi parameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP taiḥ pāśairmocayatyekaḥ śivo jīvairupāsitaḥ nibadhnāti paśūnekaścaturviṃśatipāśakaiḥ  LiP sa eva bhagavānrudro mocayatyapi sevitaḥ daśendriyamayaiḥ pāśairantaḥ karaṇasaṃbhavaiḥ  LiP bhūtatanmātrapāśaiśca paśūnmocayati prabhuḥ indriyārthamayaiḥ pāśair baddhvā viṣayinaḥ prabhuḥ  LiP āśu bhaktā bhavantyevaṃ parameśvarasevayā bhaja ityeṣa dhātur vai sevāyāṃ parikīrtitaḥ  LiP tasmātsevā budhaiḥ proktā bhaktiśabdena bhūyasī brahmadistaṃbaparyantaṃ paśūnbaddhvā maheśvaraḥ  LiP tribhirguṇamayaiḥ pāśaiḥ kāryaṃ kārayati svayam dṛḍhena bhaktiyogena paśubhiḥ samupāsitaḥ  LiP mocayatyeva tānsadyaḥ śaṅkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ bhajanaṃ bhaktirityuktā vāṅmanaḥ kāyakarmabhiḥ  LiP sarvakāryeṇahetutvātpāśacchedapaṭīyasī satyaḥ sarvaga ityādi śivasya guṇacintanā  LiP rupopādānacintā ca mānasaṃ bhajanaṃ viduḥ vācikaṃ bhajanaṃ dhīrāḥ praṇavādijapaṃ viduḥ  LiP kāyikaṃ bhajanaṃ sadbhiḥ prāṇāyāmādi kathyate dharmādharmamayaiḥ pāśairbandhanaṃ dehināmidam  LiP mocakaḥ śiva evaiko bhagavānparameśvaraḥ caturviśatitattvāni māyākarmaguṇā iti  LiP kīrtyante viṣayāśceti pāśā jīvanibandhanāt tairbaddhāḥ śivabhaktyaiva mucyante sarvadehinaḥ  LiP pañcakleśamayaiḥ pāśaiḥ paśūnbadhnāti śaṅkaraḥ sa eva mocakastoṣāṃ bhaktyā samyagupāsitaḥ  LiP avidyāmasmitāṃ rāgaṃ dveṣaṃ ca dvipadāṃ varāḥ vadantyabhiniveśaṃ ca kleśānpāśatvamāgatān  LiP tamomohomahāmohastāmisra iti paṇḍitāḥ andhatāmisra ityāhuravidyāṃ pañcadhā sthitām  LiP tāñjīvānmuniśārdūlāḥ sarvāṃścaivāpyavidyayā śivo mocayati avidyayāsya saṃbandho nātīto nāstyanāgataḥ bhavedrāgeṇa devasya śaṃbhoraṅganivāsinaḥ  LiP kāleṣu triṣu saṃbandhastasya dveṣeṇa no bhavet māyātītasya devasya sthāṇoḥ paśupatervibhoḥ  LiP sarveṣāmanukaṃpayā  LiP sa hovācaiva yājñavalkyo yadakṣaraṃ gārgyayoginaḥ abhivadanti sthūlamanantaṃ mahāścaryamadīrghamalohitamamastakamāsāyamata evo bhagavannandikeśvara  LiP śailādiruvācasanatkumāra saṃkṣepāttava vakṣyāmyaśeṣataḥ mahimānaṃ maheśasya bhavasya parameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP nāsya prakṛtibandho bhūdbuddhibandho na kaścana na cāhaṅkārabandhaśca surāḥ sarve rājānaśca maharddhikāḥ mānavā munayaścaiva sarve liṅgaṃ yajanti ca  LiP viṣṇunā rāvaṇaṃ hatvā sasainyaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sutam sthāpitaṃ vidhivadbhaktyā liṅgaṃ tīre nadīpateḥ  LiP kṛtvā pāpasahasrāṇi hatvā vipraśataṃ tathā bhāvātsamāśrito rudraṃ mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  LiP sarve liṅgamayā lokāḥ sarve liṅge pratiṣṭhitāḥ tasmādabhyarcayelliṅgaṃ yadīcchecchāśvataṃ padam  LiP sarvākārau sthitāvetau naraiḥ śreyo rthibhiḥ śivau pūjanīyau namaskāryau cintanīyau ca sarvadā  LiP iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ekādaśo dhyāyaḥsanatkumāra uvācamūrtayo ṣṭhau mamācakṣvaśaṅkarasya mahātmanaḥ viśvarūpasya devasya gaṇeśvara mahāmate  LiP nandikeśvara uvācahanta te kathayiṣyāmi mahimānamumāpateḥ viśvarūpasya devasya sarojabhavasaṃbhava  LiP bhūr āpo ḥgnir marud vyoma bhāskaro dīkṣitaḥ śaśī bhavasya mūrtayaḥ proktāḥ śivasya parameṣṭhanaḥ  LiP khātmenduvahnisūryāṃbhodharāḥ pavana ityapi tasyāṣṭa mūrtayaḥ proktā devadevasya dhīmataḥ  LiP agnihotrerpite tena sūryātmani mahātmani tadvibhūtistathā sarve devāstṛpyanti sarvadāḥ  LiP vṛkṣasya mūlasekena yathā śākhopaśākhikāḥ tathā tasyārcayā devās tathā syus tadvibhūtayaḥ  LiP tasya dvādaśadhā bhinnaṃ rūpaṃ sūryātmakaṃ prabhoḥ sarvadevātmakaṃ yājyaṃ yajānti munipuṅgavāḥ  LiP amṛtākhyā kalā tasya sarvasyādityarūpiṇaḥ bhūtasaṃjīvanī ceṣṭā lokosmin pīyate sadā  LiP candrākhyakiraṇāstasya dhūrjaṭerbhāskarātmanaḥ oṣadhīnāṃ vivṛddhyarthaṃ himavṛṣṭiṃ vitanvate  LiP suklākhyāraśmayastasya śaṃbhormārtaṇḍarūpiṇaḥ dharmaṃ vitanvate loke sasyapākādikāraṇam  LiP divākarātmanastasya harikeśāhvayaḥ karaḥ nakṣatrapoṣakaścaiva prasiddhaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP viśvakarmāhvayastasya kiraṇo budhapoṣakaḥ sarveśvarasya devasya saptasaptisvarūpiṇaḥ  LiP viśvavyaca iti khyātaḥ kiraṇastasya śūlinaḥ śukrapoṣakabhāvena pratītaḥ sūryarūpiṇaḥ  LiP saṃyadvasurīti khyāto yasya raśmistriśūlinaḥ lohitāṅgaṃ prapuṣṇāti sahasrakiraṇātmanaḥ  LiP arvāvasurīti khyāto raśmistasya pinākinaḥ bṛhaspatiṃ prapuṣṇāti sarvadā tapanātmanaḥ  LiP svarāḍiti samākhyātaḥ śivasyāṃśuḥ śanaiścaram haridaśvātmanastasya prapuṣṇāti divāniśam  LiP sūryātmakasya devasya viśvayonerumāpateḥ suṣumṇākhyaḥ sadā raśmiḥ puṣṇāti śiśiradyutim  LiP saumyānāṃ vasujātānāṃ prakṛtitvamupāgatā tasya somāhvayā mūrtiḥ śaṅkarasya jagadguroḥ  LiP tasya somātmaka rūpa śukratvena vyavasthitam śarīrabhājāṃ sarveṣāṃ devasyāntakaśāsinaḥ  LiP śarīriṇāmaśeṣāṇāṃ manasyeva vyavasthitam vapuḥ somātmakaṃ śaṃbhostasya sarvajagadguroḥ  LiP śaṃbhoḥ ṣoḍaśadhābhinnā sthitāmṛtakalātmanaḥ sarvabhūtaśarīreṣu somākhyā mūrtiruttamā  LiP devānpitṝṃś ca puṣṇāti sudhayāmṛtayā sadā mūrtiḥ somāhvayā tasya devadevasya śāsituḥ  LiP puṣṇātyoṣadhijātāni dehināmātmaśuddhaye somāhvayā tanustasya bhavānīmiti nirdiśet  LiP yajñānāṃ patibhāvena jīvānāṃ tapasāmapi prasiddharūpametadvai momātmakamumāpateḥ  LiP jalānāmoṣadhīnāṃ ca patibhāvena viśrutam somātmakaṃ vapustasya śaṃbhorbhagavataḥ prabhoḥ  LiP devo hiraṇmayo mṛṣṭaḥ parasparavivekinaḥ karaṇānāmaśeṣāṇāṃ devatānāṃ nirākṛtiḥ  LiP jīvatvena sthite tasmiñchive somātmake prabhau madhurā vilayaṃ yāti sarvalokaikarakṣiṇī  LiP yajamānāhvayā mūrtiḥ śaivī havyairaharniśam puṣṇāti devatāḥ sarvāḥ kavyaiḥ pitṛgaṇānapi  LiP yajamānāhvayā yā sā tanuścāhutijā tayā vṛṣṭyā bhāvayati spaṣṭaṃ sarvameva parāparam  LiP antaḥsthaṃ ca bahiḥsthaṃ ca brahmāṇḍānāṃ sthitaṃ jalam bhūtānāṃ ca śarīrasthaṃ śaṃbhormūrtirgarīyasī  LiP nadīnāmamṛtaṃ sākṣānnadānāmapi sarvadā samudrāṇāṃ ca sarvatra vyāpī sarvamumāpatiḥ  LiP saṃjīvinī samastānāṃ bhūtānāmeva pāvinī aṃbikā prāṇasaṃsthā yā mūrtilaṃbumayī parā  LiP antaḥsthaś ca bahiḥsthaś ca brahmāṇḍānāṃ vibhāvasuḥ yajñānāṃ ca śarīrasthaḥ śaṃbhormūrtirgarīyasī  LiP śarīrasthā ca bhūtānāṃ śreyasī mūrtiraiśvarī mūrtiḥ pāvaka saṃsthā yā śaṃbhoratyantapūjitā  LiP bhedā ekonapañcāśadvedavidbhirudāhṛtāḥ havyaṃ vahati devānāṃ śaṃbhoryajñātmakaṃ vapuḥ  LiP kavyaṃ pitṛgaṇānāṃ ca hūyamānaṃ dvijātibhiḥ sarvadevamayaṃ śaṃbhoḥ śreṣṭhamagyātmakaṃ vapuḥ  LiP vadanti vedaśāstrajñā yajanti ca yathāvidhi antaḥstho jagadaṇḍānāṃ bahiḥsthaśca samīraṇaḥ  LiP śarīrasthaśca bhūtānāṃ śaivī mūrtiḥ paṭīyasī prāṇādyā nāgakūrmādyā āvahādyāśca vāyavaḥ  LiP īśānamūrterekasya bhedāḥ sarve prakīrtitāḥ antaḥsthaṃ jagadaṇḍānāṃ bahiḥsthaṃ ca viyadvibhoḥ  LiP śarīrasthaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ śaṃbhomūrtirgarīyasī śaṃbhorviśvaṃbharā mūrtiḥ sarvabrahmādhidevatā  LiP carācarāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ sarveṣāṃ dhāraṇe matā carācarāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ śarīrāṇi vidurbudhāḥ  LiP pañcakenesamūrtīnāṃ samārabdhāni sarvathā pañcabhūtāni candrārkāvātmeti munipuṅgavāḥ  LiP mūrtayo ṣṭau śivasyāhurdevadevasya dhīmataḥ ātmā tasyāṣṭamī mūrtiryajamānāhvayā parā  LiP carācara śarīreṣu sarveṣveva sthitā tadā dīkṣitaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ prāhurātmānaṃ ca munīśvarāḥ  LiP yajamānāhvayā mūrtiḥ śivasya śivadāyinaḥ mūrtayo ṣṭau śivasyaitā vandanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ  LiP śreyo ḥrthibhir narair nityaṃ śreyasāmekahetavaḥ  LiP iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge dvādaśo dhyāyaḥsanatkumāra uvācabhūyo pi vada me nandin mahimānamumāpate aṣṭamūrtermaheśasya śivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP nandikeśvara uvācavakṣyāmi te maheśasya mahimānamumāpateḥ aṣṭamūrterjagadvyāpya sthitasya parameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP carācarāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ dhātā viśvaṃbharātmakaḥ śarva ityucyate devaḥ sarvaśāstrārthapāragaiḥ  LiP viśvaṃbharātmanastasya sarvasya parameṣṭhinaḥ vikeśī kathyate patnī tanayoṅgārakaḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP bhava ityucyate devo bhagavānvedavādibhiḥ saṃjīvanasya lokānāṃ bhavasya paramātmanaḥ  LiP umā saṃkīrtitā devī sutaḥ śukraśca sūribhiḥ saptalokāṇḍakavyāpī sarvalokaikarakṣitā  LiP vahnyātmā bhagavāndevaḥ smṛtaḥ paśupatirbudhaiḥ svāhā patnyātmanastasya proktā paśupateḥ priyā  LiP ṣaṇmukho bhagavān devo budhaiḥ putra udāhṛtaḥ samastabhuvanavyāpī bhartā sarvaśarīriṇām  LiP pavanātmā budhairdeva īśāna iti kīrtyate īśānasya jagatkarturdevasya pavanātmanaḥ  LiP śivā devī budairuktā putraścāsya manojavaḥ carācarāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ sarveṣāṃ sarvakāmadaḥ  LiP vyomātmā bhagavāndevo bhīma ityucyate budhaiḥ mahāmahimno devasya bhīmasya gaganātmanaḥ  LiP diśo daśa smṛtā devyaḥ sutaḥ sargaśca sūribhiḥ sūryātmā bhagavāndevaḥ sarveṣāṃ ca vibhūtidaḥ  LiP rudra ityucyate devairbhagavān bhuktimuktidaḥ sūryātma kasya rudrasya bhaktānāṃ bhaktidāyinaḥ  LiP suvarcalā smṛtā devī sutaścāsya śanaiścaraḥ samastasaumyavastūnāṃ prakṛtitvena viśrutaḥ  LiP somātmako budhairdevo mahādeva iti smṛtaḥ somātmakasya devasya mahādevasya sūribhiḥ  LiP dayitā rohiṇī proktā budhaścaiva śarīrajaḥ havyakavyasthitiṃ kurvan havyakavyāśināṃ tadā  LiP yajamānātmako devo mahādevo budhaiḥ prabhuḥ ugra ityucyate sadbhirīśānaśceti cāparaiḥ  LiP ugrāhvayasya devasya yajamānātmanaḥ prabhoḥ dīkṣā patnī budhairuktā saṃtānākhyaḥ sutastathā  LiP śarīriṇāṃ śarīreṣu kaṭhinaṃ koṅkaṇādivat pārthivaṃ tadvapurjñeyaṃ śarvatattvaṃ bubhutsubhiḥ  LiP dehedehe tu deveśo dehabhājāṃ yadavyayam vastudravyātmakaṃ tasya bhavasya paramātmanaḥ  LiP jñeyaṃ ca tattvavidbhirvai sarvavedārthapāragaiḥ āgneyaḥ pariṇāmo yo vigraheṣu śarīriṇām  LiP mūrtiḥ paśupatirjñeyā sā tattvaṃ vettumicchubhiḥ vāyavyaḥ pariṇāmo yaḥ śarīreṣu śarīriṇām  LiP budhairīśoti sā tasya tanurjñeyā na saṃśayaḥ suṣiraṃ yaccharīrasthamaśeṣāṇāṃ śarīriṇām  LiP bhīmasya sā tanurjñeyā tattvavijñānakāṅkṣibhiḥ cakṣurādigataṃ tejo yaccharīrasthamaṅginām  LiP rudrasyāpi tanurjñeyā paramārthaṃ bubhutsubhiḥ sarvabhūtaśarīreṣu manaścandrātmakaṃ hi yat  LiP mahādevasya sā mūrtirboddhavyā tattvacintakaiḥ ātmā yo yajamānākhyaḥ sarvabhūtaśarīragaḥ  LiP mūrtirugrasya sā jñeyā paramātmabubhutsubhiḥ jātānāṃ sarva bhūtānāṃ caturdaśasu yoniṣu  LiP aṣṭamūrterananyatvaṃ vadanti paramarṣayaḥ saptamūrtimayānyāhurīśasyāṅgāni dehinām  LiP ātmā tasyāṣṭamī mūrtiḥ sarvabhūtaśarīragā aṣṭamūrtimamuṃ devaṃ sarvalokātmakaṃ vibhum  LiP bhajasva sarvabhāvena śreyaḥ prāptuṃ yadīcchasi prāṇino yasya kasyāpi kriyate yadyanugrahaḥ  LiP aṣṭamūrtermaheśasya kṛtamārādhanaṃ bhavet nigrahaścet kṛto loke dehino yasya kasyacit  LiP aṣṭamūrtermaheśasya sa eva vihito bhavet yadyavajñā kṛtā loke yasya kasya cidaṅginaḥ  LiP aṣṭamūrtermahe śasya vihitā sā bhavedvibhoḥ abhayaṃ yat pradattaṃ syādaṅgino vasya kasyacit  LiP ārādhanaṃ kṛtaṃ tasmādaṣṭamūrterna saṃśayaḥ sarvopakārakaraṇaṃ pradānamabhayasya ca  LiP ārādhanaṃ tu devasya aṣṭamūrterna saṃśayaḥ sarvopakārakaraṇaṃ sarvānugraha eva ca  LiP tadarcanaṃ paraṃ prāhuraṣṭamūrtermunīśvarāḥ anugrahaṇamanyeṣāṃ vidhātavyaṃ tvayāṅginām  LiP sarvābhayapradānaṃ ca śivārādhanamicchatā  LiP iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge trayodaśo dhyāyaḥsanatkumāra uvācapañca brahmāṇi me nandinnācakṣva gaṇasattama śreyaḥkaraṇabhūtāni pavitrāṇi śarīriṇām  LiP nandikeśvara uvācaśivasyaiva svarūpāṇi pañca brahmāhvayāni te kathayāmi yathātattvaṃ padmayoneḥ sutottama  LiP sarvalokaikasaṃhartā sarvalokaikarakṣitā sarvalokaikanirmātā pañcabrahmātmakaḥ śaviḥ  LiP sarveṣāmeva lokānāṃ yadupādānakāraṇam nimittakāraṇaṃ cāhussa śivaḥ pañcadhā smṛtaḥ  LiP mūrtayaḥ pañca vikhyātāḥ pañca brahmāhvayāḥ parāḥ sarvalokaśaraṇyasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ  LiP kṣetrajñaḥ prathamā mūrtiśivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ bhoktā prakṛtivargasya bhogyasyeśānasaṃjñitaḥ  LiP sthāṇostatpuruṣākhyā ca dvitīyā mūrtirucyate prakṛtiḥ sā hi vijñeyā paramātmaguhātmikā  LiP aghorākhyā tṛtīyā ca śaṃbhormūrtirgarīyasī buddheḥ sā mūrtirityuktā dharmādyaṣṭāṅgasaṃyutā  LiP caturthī vāmadevākhyā mūrtiḥ śaṃbhorgariyasī ahaṅkārātmakatvena vyāpya sarvaṃ vyavasthitā  LiP sadyojātāhvayā śaṃbhoḥ pacamī mūrtirucyate manastattvātmakatvena sthitā sarvaśarīriṣu  LiP īśānaḥ paramo devaḥ parameṣṭhī sanātanaḥ śrotrendriyātmakatvena sarvabhūteṣvavasthitaḥ  LiP sthitastatpuruṣo devaḥ śarīreṣu śarīriṇām tvagindriyātmakatvena tattvavidbhirudāhṛtaḥ  LiP aghoropi mahādevaścakṣurātmatayā budhaiḥ kīrtitaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ śarīreṣu vyavasthitaḥ  LiP jihvendriyātmakatvena vāmadevopi viśrutaḥ aṅgabhājāmaśeṣāṇāmaṅgeṣuṃ paridhiṣṭhitaḥ  LiP ghrāṇendriyātmakatvena sadyojātaḥ smṛto budhaiḥ prāṇabhājāṃ samastānāṃ vigraheṣu vyavasthitaḥ  LiP sarveṣveva śarīreṣu prāṇabhājāṃ pratiṣṭhitaḥ vāgindriyātmakatvena budhairīśāna ucyate  LiP pāṇīndriyātmakatvena sthitastatpuruṣo budhaiḥ ucyate vigraheṣveva sarvavigrahadhāriṇām  LiP sarvavigrahiṇāṃ dehe hyaghoropi vyavasthitaḥ pādendriyātmakatvena kīrtitas tattvavedibhiḥ  LiP pāyvindriyātmakatvena vāmadevo vyavasthitaḥ sarvabhūtanikāyānāṃ kāyeṣu munibhiḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP upasthātmatayā devaḥ sadyojātaḥ sthitaḥ prabhuḥ iṣyate vedaśāstrajñairdeheṣu prāṇadhāriṇām  LiP īśānaṃ prāṇināṃ devaṃ śabdatanmātrarūpiṇam ākāśajanakaṃ prāhurmunivṛndārakaprajāḥ  LiP prāhustatpuruṣaṃ devaṃ sparśatanmātrakātmakam samīrajanakaṃ prāhurbhagavantaṃ munīśvarāḥ  LiP rūpatanmātrakaṃ devamaghoramapi ghorakam prāhurvedavido mukhyā janakaṃ jātavedasaḥ  LiP rasatanmātrarūpatvāt prathitaṃ tattvavedinaḥ vāmadevamapāṃ prāhurjanakatvena saṃsthitam  LiP sadyojātaṃ mahādevaṃ gandhatanmātrarūpiṇam bhūmyātmānaṃ praśaṃsaṃti sarvatattvārthavedinaḥ  LiP ākāśātmānamīśānamādidevaṃ munīśvarāḥ parameṇa mahattvena saṃbhūtaṃ prāhuradbhutam  LiP prabhuṃ tatpuruṣaṃ devaṃ pavanaṃ pavanātmakam samastalokavyāpitvātprathitaṃ sūrayo viduḥ  LiP athārcitatayā khyātamaghoraṃ dahanātmakam kathayanti mahātmānaṃ vedavākyārthavedinaḥ  LiP toyātmakaṃ mahādevaṃ vāmadevaṃ manoramaṃm jagatsaṃjīvanatvena kathitaṃ munayo viduḥ  LiP viśvaṃbharātmakaṃ devaṃ sadyojātaṃ jagadgurum carācarekabhartāraṃ paraṃ kavivarā viduḥ  LiP pañcabrahmātmakaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam śivānandaṃ tadityāhurmunayastattvadarśinaḥ  LiP pañcaviṃśatitattvātmā prapañce yaḥ pradṛśyate pañcabrahmātmakatvena sa śivo nānyatāṃ gataḥ  LiP pañcaviṃśatitattvātmā pañcabrahmātmakaḥ śivaḥ śreyorthibhirato nityaṃ cintanīyaḥ prayatnataḥ  LiP iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge pañcabrahmakathanaṃ nāma caturdaśo dhyāyaḥsanatkumāra uvācabhūyo pi śivamāhātmyaṃ samācakṣva mahāmate sarvajño hyasi bhūtānā madhinātha mahāguṇa  LiP śailādiruvācaśivamāhātmyamekāgraḥ śṛṇu vakṣyāmi te mune bahubhirbahudhā śabdaiḥ kīrtitaṃ munisattamaiḥ  LiP sadasadrūpamityāhuḥ sadasatpatirityapi taṃ śivaṃ munayaḥ kecitpravadanti ca sūrayaḥ  LiP bhūtabhāvavikāreṇa dvitīyena sa ucyate vyaktaṃ tena vihīnatvādavyaktamasadityapi  LiP ubhe te śivarūpe hi śivādanyaṃ na vidyate tayoḥ patitvācca śivaḥ sadasatpatirucyate  LiP kṣarākṣarātmakaṃ prāhuḥ kṣarākṣaraparaṃ tathā śivaṃ maheśvaraṃ kecinmunayastattvacintakāḥ  LiP uktamakṣaramavyaktaṃ vyaktaṃ kṣaramudāhṛtam rūpe te śaṅkarasyaiva tasmānna para ucyate  LiP tayoḥ paraḥ śivaḥ śāntaḥ kṣarākṣaraparo budhaiḥ ucyate paramārthena mahādevo maheśvaraḥ  LiP samastavyaktarūpaṃ tu tataḥ smṛtvā sa mucyate samaṣṭivyaṣṭirūpaṃ tu samaṣṭivyaṣṭikāraṇam  LiP vadanti kecidācāryāḥ śivaṃ paramakāraṇam samaṣṭiṃ viduravyaktaṃ vyaṣṭiṃ vyaktaṃ munīśvarāḥ  LiP rūpe te gadite śaṃbhornāstyanyadvastusaṃbhavam tayoḥ kāramabhāvena śivo hi parameśvaraḥ  LiP ucyate yogaśāstrajñaiḥ samaṣṭivyaṣṭikāraṇam kṣetrakṣetrajñarūpī ca śivaḥ kaiścidudāhṛtaḥ  LiP paramātmā paraṃ jyotirbhagavānparameśvaraḥ caturviśatitattvāni samaṣṭivyaṣṭikāraṇam  LiP prāhuḥ kṣetrajñaśabdena bhoktāraṃ puruṣaṃ tathā kṣetrakṣetravidāvete rūpe tasya svayaṃbhuvaḥ  LiP na kiñcicca śivādanyaditi prāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ aparabrahmarūpaṃ taṃ parabrahmātmakaṃ śivam  LiP kecidāhurmahādevamanādi nidhanaṃ prabhum bhūtendriyāntaḥ karaṇapradhānaviṣayātmakam  LiP aparaṃ brahma nirdiṣṭaṃ paraṃ brahma cidātmakam brahmaṇī te maheśasya śivasyāsya svayaṃbhuvaḥ  LiP śaṅkarasya parasyaiva śivādanyanna vidyate vidyāvidyāsvarūpī ca śaṅkaraḥ kaiściducyate  LiP dhātā vidhātā lokānāmādidevo maheśvaraḥ vidyeti ca tamevāhuravidyeti munīśvarāḥ  LiP prapañcajātamakhilaṃ te svarūpe svayaṃbhuvaḥ bhrāntirvidyā paraṃ ceti śivarūpamanuttamam  LiP avāpurmunayo yogātkecidāgamavedinaḥ artheṣu bahurūpeṣu vijñānaṃ bhrāntirucyate  LiP ātmākāreṇa saṃvittirbudhairvidyeti kīrtyate vikalparahitaṃ tattvaṃ paramityabhidhīyate  LiP tṛtīyarūpamīśasya nānyatkiñcana sarvataḥ vyaktāvyaktajñarūpīti śivaḥ kaiścinnigadyate  LiP vidhātā sarva lokānāṃ dhātā ca parameśvaraḥ trayoviṃśatitattvāni vyaktaśabdena sūrayaḥ  LiP vadantyavyaktaśabdena prakṛtiḥ ca parāṃ tathā kathayanti jñaśabdena puruṣaṃ gumabhoginam  LiP tattrayaṃ śāṅkaraṃ rūpaṃ nānyatkiñcidaśāṅkaram  LiP iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge pañcadaśo dhyāyaḥsanatkumāra uvācapunareva mahābuddhe śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ bahubhirbahudhā śabdaiḥ śabditāni munīśvaraiḥ  LiP śailādiruvācapunaḥ punaḥ pravakṣyāmi śivarūpāṇi te mune bahubhirbahudhā śabdaiḥ śabditāni munīśvaraiḥ  LiP kṣetrajñaḥ prakṛtirvyaktaṃ kālātmeti munīśvaraiḥ ucyate kaiścidācāryairāgamārṇavapāragaiḥ  LiP kṣetrajñaṃ puruṣaṃ prāhuḥ pradhānaṃ prakṛtiṃ budhāḥ vikārajātaṃ niḥśeṣaṃ prakṛtervyaktamityapi  LiP pradhānavyaktayoḥ kālaḥ pariṇāmaikakāraṇam taccatuṣṭayamīśasya rūpāṇāṃ hi catuṣṭayam  LiP hiraṇyagarbhaṃ puruṣaṃ pradhānaṃ vyaktarūpiṇam kathayanti śivaṃ kecidācāryāḥ parameśvaram  LiP hiraṇyagarbhaḥ kartāsya bhoktā viśvasya pūruṣaḥ vikārajātaṃ vyaktākhyaṃ pradhānaṃ kāraṇaṃ param  LiP teṣāṃ catuṣṭayaṃ buddheḥ śivarūpacatuṣṭayam procyate śaṅkarādanyadasti vastu na kiñcana  LiP piṇḍajātisvarūpī tu kathyate kauścidīśvaraḥ carācaraśarīrāṇi piṇḍākhyāny akhilāny api  LiP sāmānyāni samastāni mahāsāmānyameva ca kathyante jātiśabdena tāni rūpāṇi dhīmataḥ  LiP virāṭ hiraṇyagarbhātmā kaiścidīśo nigadyate hiraṇyagarbho lokānāṃ heturlokātmako virāṭ  LiP sūtrāvyākṛtarūpaṃ taṃ śivaṃ śaṃsaṃti kecana avyākṛtaṃ pradhānaṃ hi tadrūpaṃ parameṣṭhanaḥ  LiP lokā yenaiva tiṣṭhanti sūtre maṇigaṇā iva tatsūtramiti vijñeyaṃ rūpamadbhutavikramam  LiP antaryāmī paraḥ kaiścitkaiścidīśaḥ prakīrtyate svayañjyotiḥ svayaṃvedyaḥ śivaḥ śaṃbhurmaheśvaraḥ  LiP sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāmantaryāmī śivaḥ smṛtaḥ sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ paratvātpara ucyate  LiP paramātmā śivaḥ śaṃbhuḥ śaṅkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ prājñataijasaviśvākhyaṃ tasya rūpatrayaṃ viduḥ  LiP suṣuptisvapnajāgrantamavasthātrayameva tat virāṭ hiraṇyagarbhākhyamavyākṛtapadāhvayam  LiP turīyasya śivasyāsya avasthātrayagāminaḥ hiraṇyagarbhaḥ puruṣaḥ kāla ity eva kīrtitāḥ  LiP tisro vasthā jagatsṛṣṭisthitisaṃhārahetavaḥ bhavaviṣṇuviriñcākhyamavasthātrayamīśituḥ  LiP ārādhya bhaktyā muktiṃ ca prāpnuvanti śarīriṇaḥ kartā kriyā ca kāryaṃ ca karaṇaṃ ceti sūribhiḥ  LiP śaṃbhoścatvāri rūpāṇi kīrtyante parameṣṭhinaḥ pramātā ca pramāṇaṃ ca prameyaṃ pramitistathā  LiP catvāryetāni rūpāṇi śivasyaiva na saṃśayaḥ īśvarāvyākṛtaprāṇavirāṭbhūtendriyātmakam  LiP śivasyaiva vikāro yaṃ samudrasyeva vīcayaḥ īśvaraṃ jagatāmāhurnimittaṃ kāraṇaṃ tathā  LiP avyākṛtaṃ pradhānaṃ hi taduktaṃ vedavādibhiḥ hiraṇyagarbhaḥ prāṇākhyo virāṭ lokātmakaḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP mahā bhūtāni bhūtāni kāryāṇi indriyāṇi ca śivasyaitāni rūpāṇi śaṃsaṃti munisattamāḥ  LiP paramātmā śivādanyo nāstīti kavayoviduḥ śivajātāni tattvāni pañcaviṃśanmanīṣibhiḥ  LiP uktāni na tadanyāni salilādūrmivṛndavat pañcaviṃśatpadārthebhyaḥ śivatattvaṃ paraṃ viduḥ  LiP tāni tasmādananyāni suvarṇakaṭakādivat sadāśiveśvarādyāni tattvāni śivatattvataḥ  LiP jātāni na tadanyāni mṛddravyaṃ kuṃbhabhedavat māyā vidyā kriyā śaktirjñānaśaktiḥ kriyāmayī  LiP jātāḥ śivānna saṃdehaḥ kiraṇā iva sūryataḥ sarvātmakaṃ śivaṃ devaṃ sarvāśrayavidhāyinam  LiP bhajasva sarvabhāvena śreyaścetprāptumicchasi  LiP iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ṣoḍaśo dhyāyaḥsanatkumāra uvācabhūyo devagaṇaśreṣṭha śivamāhātmyamuttamam śṛṇvato nāsti me tṛptistva dvākyāmṛtapānataḥ  LiP kathaṃ śarīrī bhagavān kasmādrudraḥ pratāpavān sarvātmā ca kathaṃ śambhuḥ kathaṃ pāśupataṃ vratam  LiP kathaṃ vā devamukhyaiśca śruto dṛṣṭaśca śaṅkaraḥ śailādiruvācaavyaktādabhavatsthāṇuḥ śivaḥ paramakāraṇam  LiP sa sarvakāraṇopeta ṛpirviśvāvikaḥ prabhuḥ devānāṃ prathamaṃ devaṃ jāyamānaṃ mukhāmbujāt  LiP dadarśa cāgre brahmāṇaṃ cājñayā tamavaikṣata dṛṣṭo rudreṇa deveśaḥ sasarja sakalaṃ ca saḥ  LiP varṇāśramavyavasthāśca sthāpayāmāsa vai virāṭ somaṃ sasarja yajñārthaṃ somādidamajāyata  LiP caruśca vahniryajñaśca vajrapāṇiḥ śacīpatiḥ viṣṇurnārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān sarvaṃ somamayaṃ jagat  LiP rudrādhyāyena te devā rudraṃ tuṣṭuvurīśvaram prasannavadanastasthau devānāṃ madhyataḥ prabhuḥ  LiP apahṛtya ca vijñānameṣāmeva maheśvaraḥ devā hyapṛcchaṃstaṃ devaṃ ko bhavāniti śaṅkaram  LiP abravīdbhagavānrudro hyahamekaḥ purātanaḥ āsaṃ prathama evāhaṃ vartāmi ca surottamāḥ  LiP bhaviṣyāmi ca loke sminmatto nānyaḥ kutaścana vyatiriktaṃ na matto sti nānyatkiñcitsurottamāḥ  LiP nityo nityo hamanagho brāhmāhaṃ brahmaṇaspatiḥ diśaśca vidiśaścāhaṃ prakṛtiśca pumānaham  LiP triṣṭubjagatyanuṣṭup ca cchandohaṃ tanmayaḥ śivaḥ satyohaṃ sarvagaḥ śāntastretāgnirgauravaṃ guruḥ  LiP gaurahaṃ gahvaraścāhaṃ nityaṃ gahanagocaraḥ jyeṣṭhohaṃ sarvatattvānāṃ variṣṭhohamapāṃ patiḥ  LiP āpohaṃ bhagavānīśastejohaṃ vedirapyaham ṛgvedohaṃ yajurvedaḥ sāmavedohamātmabhūḥ  LiP atharvaṇohaṃ mantrohaṃ tathā cāṅgirasāṃ varaḥ itihāsapurāṇāni kalpohaṃ kalpanāpyaham  LiP akṣaraṃ ca kṣaraṃ cāhaṃ kṣāntiḥ śāntirahaṃ kṣamā guhyohaṃ sarvavedeṣu vareṇyohamajopyaham  LiP puṣkaraṃ ca pavitraṃ ca madhyaṃ cāhaṃ tataḥ param bahiścāhaṃ tathā cāntaḥ purastādahamavyayaḥ  LiP jyotiścāhaṃ tamaścāhaṃ brahmā viṣṇurmaheśvaraḥ buddhiścāhamahaṅkārastanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi ca  LiP evaṃ sarvaṃ ca māmeva yo veda sura sattamāḥ sa eva sarvavitsarvaṃ sarvātmā parameśvaraḥ  LiP gāṃ gobhirbrāhmaṇānsarvānbrahmaṇyena havīṃṣi ca āyuṣāyustathā satyaṃ satyena surasattamāḥ  LiP dharmaṃ dharmeṇa sarvāṃśca tarpayāmi svatejasā ityādau bhagavānuktvā tatraivāntaradhīyata  LiP nāpaśyanta tato devaṃ rudraṃ paramakāraṇam te devāḥ paramātmānaṃ rudraṃ dhyāyanti śaṅkaram  LiP sanārāyaṇakā devāḥ seṃdrāśca munayastathā tathordhvabāhavo devā rudraṃ stunvanti saṃkaram  LiP iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge saptadaśo dhyāyaḥdevā ūcuḥya eṣa bhagavān rudro brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ skandaścāpi tathā cedro bhuvanāni caturdaśa aśvinau grahatārāsca nakṣatrāṇi ca khaṃ diśaḥ  LiP bhūtāni ca tathā sūryaḥ somaścāṣṭau grahāstathā prāṇaḥ kālo yamo mṛtyuramṛtaḥ parameśvaraḥ  LiP bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyacca vartamānaṃ maheśvaraḥ viśvaṃ kṛtsnaṃ jagatsarvaṃ satyaṃ tasmai namonamaḥ  LiP tvamādau ca tathā bhūto bhūrbhuvaḥ svastathaiva ca ante tvaṃ viśvarūpo si śīrṣaṃ tu jagataḥ saṃdā  LiP brahmaikastvaṃ dvitridhārthamadhaśca tvaṃ sureśvaraḥ śāntiśca tvaṃ tathā puṣṭistuṣṭiścāpyahutaṃ hutam  LiP viśvaṃ caiva tathāviśvaṃ dattaṃ vādattamīśvaram kṛtaṃ cāpyakṛtaṃ devaṃ paramapyaparaṃ dhruvam parāyaṇaṃ satāṃ caiva hyasatāmapi śaṅkaram  LiP apāma somam amṛtā abhūmāganma jyotiravidāma devān kiṃ nūnamasmānkṛṇavadarātiḥ kimu dhūrtiramṛtaṃ martyasya  LiP etajjagaddhitaṃ divyamakṣaraṃ sūkṣmamavyayam  LiP prājā patyaṃ pavitraṃ ca saumyamagrāhyamavyayam agrāhyeṇāpi vā grāhyaṃ vāyavyena samīraṇaḥ  LiP saumyena saumyaṃ grasati tejasā svena līlayā tasmai namo pasaṃhartre mahāgrāsāya śūline  LiP hṛdisthā devatāḥ sarvā hṛdi prāṇe pratiṣṭhitāḥ hṛdi tvamasi yo nityaṃ tisro mātrāḥ parastu saḥ  LiP śiraścottarataścaiva pādau dakṣiṇatastathā yo vai cottarataḥ sākṣātsa oṅkāraḥ sanātanaḥ  LiP oṅkāro yaḥ sa eveha praṇavo vyāpya tiṣṭhati anantastārasūkṣmaṃ ca śuklaṃ vaidyutameva ca  LiP paraṃ brahmā sa īśāna ekorudraḥ sa eva ca bhavānmaheśvaraḥ sākṣānmahādevo na saṃśayaḥ  LiP ūrdhvamunnāmayatyeva sa oṅkāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ prāṇānavati yastasmāt praṇavaḥ parikīrtitaḥ  LiP sarvaṃ vyāpnoti yastasmātsarvavyāpī sanātanaḥ brahmā hariśca bhagavānādyantaṃ nopalabdhavān  LiP tathānye ca tato nanto rudraḥ paramakāraṇam yastārayati saṃsārāttāra ityabhidhīyate  LiP sūkṣmo bhūtvā śarīrāṇi sarvadā hyadhitiṣṭhiti tasmātsūkṣmaḥ samākhyāto bhagavannīlalohitaḥ  LiP nīlaśca lohitaścaiva pradhānapuruṣānvayāt skandate sya yataḥ śukraṃ tathā śukramapaitica  LiP vidyotayati yastasmādvaidyutaḥ parigīyate bṛhattvādbṛṃhaṇatvācca bṛhate ca parāpare  LiP tasmādbṛṃhati yasmāddhi paraṃ brahmeti kīrtitam advitīyo tha bhagavāṃsturīyaḥ parameśvaraḥ  LiP īśānamasya jagataḥ svardṛśāṃ cakṣur īśvaram īśānamindrasūrayaḥ sarveṣāmapi sarvadā  LiP īśānaḥ sarvavidyānāṃ yattadīśāna ucyate yadīkṣate ca bhagavānnirīkṣyamiti cājñayā  LiP ātmajñānaṃ mahādevo yogaṃ gamayati svayam bhagavāṃścocyate devo devadevo maheśvaraḥ  LiP sarvāṃllokānkrameṇaiva yo gṛhṇati maheśvaraḥ visṛjatyepa deveśo vāsayatyapi līlayā  LiP eṣo hi devaḥ pradiśo nusarvāḥ pūrvo hi jātaḥ sa u garbhe antaḥ sa eva jātaḥ sa janiṣyamāṇaḥ pratyaṅmukhāstiṣṭhati sarvatomukhaḥ  LiP upāsitavyaṃ yatnena tadetatsadbhiravyayam yato vāco nivartante hyaprāpya manasā saha  LiP tadagrahaṇameveha yadvāgvadati yatnataḥ aparaṃ ca paraṃ veti parāyaṇamiti svayam  LiP vadanti vācaḥ sarvajñaḥ śaṅkaraṃ nīlalohitam eṣa sarvo namastasmai puruṣaḥ piṅgalaḥ śivaḥ  LiP sa eṣa sa mahārudro viśvaṃ bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyati bhuvanaṃ bahudhā jātaṃ jāyamānamitastataḥ  LiP hiraṇyabāhurbhagavān hiraṇyapatirīśvaraḥ aṃbikāpatirīśāno hemaretā vṛṣadhvajaḥ  LiP umāpatirvirūpākṣo viśvasṛgviśvavāhanaḥ brahmāṇaṃ vidadhe yo sau putramagre sanātanam  LiP prahiṇoti sma tasyaiva jñānamātmaprakāśakam tamekaṃ puruṣaṃ rudraṃ puruhutaṃ puruṣṭutam  LiP bālāgramātraṃ hṛdayasya madhye viśvandevaṃ vahnirūpaṃ vareṇyam tamātmasthaṃ ye nupaśyanti dhīrāsteṣāṃ śāntiḥ śāśvatī netareṣām  LiP mahato yo mahīyāṃśca hyaṇorapyaṇuravyayaḥ guhāyāṃ nihitaścātmā jantorasya maheśvaraḥ  LiP veśmabhūto sya viśvasya kamalastho hṛti svayam gahvaraṃ gahanaṃ tatsthaṃ tasyāntaścordhvataḥ sthitaḥ  LiP tatrāpi dahraṃ gaganamoṅkāraṃ parameśvaram bālāgramātraṃ tanmadhye ṛtaṃ paramakāraṇam  LiP satyaṃ brahma mahādevaṃ puruṣaṃ kṛṣṇapiṅgalam ūrdhvaratesamīśānaṃ virūpākṣamajodbhavam  LiP adhitiṣṭhati yoniṃ yo yoniṃ vācaika īśvaraḥ dehaṃ pañcavidhaṃ yena tamīśānaṃ purātanam  LiP prāṇeṣvantarmanaso liṅgamāhuryasminkrodho yā ca tṛṣṇā kṣamā ca tṛṣṇāṃ chittvā hetujālasya mūlaṃ buddhyācintyaṃ sthāpayitvā ca rudre  LiP ekaṃ tamāhurvai rudraṃ śāśvataṃ parameśvaram parātparataraṃ vāpi parātparataraṃ dhruvam  LiP brahmaṇo janakaṃ viṣṇorvahnervāyoḥ sadāśivam dhyātvāgninā ca śodhyāṅgaṃ viśodhya ca pṛthakpṛthak  LiP pañcabhūtāni saṃyamya mātrāvidhiguṇakramāt mātrāḥ pañca catasraśca trimātrādistataḥ param  LiP ekamātramamātraṃ hi dvādaśānte vyavasthitam sthitvā sthāpyāmṛto bhūtvā vrataṃ pāśupataṃ caret  LiP etadvrataṃ pāśupataṃ cariṣyāmi samāsataḥ agnimādhāya vidhivadṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃbhavaiḥ  LiP upoṣitaḥ śuciḥ snātaḥ śuklāṃbaradharaḥ svayam śuklayajñopavīti ca śuklamālyānulepanaḥ  LiP juhuyādvirajovidvān virajāśca bhaviṣyati vāyavaḥ pañca śudhyatāṃ vāṅmanaścaraṇādayaḥ  LiP śrotraṃ jihvā tataḥ prāṇastato buddhistathaiva ca śiraḥ pāṇistathā pārśvaṃ pṛṣṭhodaramanantaram  LiP jaṅghe śiśramupasthaṃ ca pāyurmeḍhraṃ tathaiva ca tvacā māṃsaṃ ca rudhiraṃ medo sthīni tathaiva ca  LiP śabdaḥ sparśaṃ ca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhastathaiva ca bhūtāni caiva śudhyantāṃ dehe medādayastathā  LiP annaṃ prāṇe mano jñānaṃ śudhyantāṃ vai śivecchayā hutvājyena samidbhiśca caruṇā ca yathākramam  LiP upasaṃhṛtya rudrāgniṃ gṛhītvā bhasma yatnataḥ agnirityādinā dhīmān vimṛjyāṅgāni saṃspṛśet  LiP etatpāśupataṃ divyaṃ vrataṃ pāśavimocanam brāhmaṇānāṃ hitaṃ proktaṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ tathaiva ca  LiP vaiśyānāmapi yogyānāṃ yatīnāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ vānaprasthāśramasthānāṃ gṛhasthānāṃ satāmapi  LiP vimuktirvidhinānena dṛṣṭvā vai brahmacāriṇām agnirityādinā bhasma gṛhītvā hyagnihotrajam  LiP so pi pāśupato vipro vimṛjyāṅgāni saṃspṛśet bhasmācchanno dvijo vidvān mahāpātakasaṃbhavaiḥ  LiP pāpaurvimucyate sadyo mucyate ca na saṃśayaḥ vīryamagreryato bhasma vīryavānbhasmasaṃyutaḥ  LiP bhasmāsnānarato vipro bhasmaśāyī jitendriyaḥ sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt  LiP tasmātsarvaprayatnena bhūtyaṅgaṃ pūjayedvudhaḥ rerekāro na kartavyastuntuṅkārastathaiva ca  LiP na tatkṣamati deveśo brahmā vā yadi keśavaḥ mama putro bhasmadhārī gaṇeśaśca varānane  LiP teṣāṃ viruddhaṃ yattyājyaṃ sa yāti narakārṇavam gṛhastho brahmahīnopi tripuṇḍraṃ yo na kārayet  LiP pūjā karma kriyā tasya dānaṃ snānaṃ tathaiva ca niṣphalaṃ jāyate sarvaṃ yathā bhasmani vai hutam  LiP tasmācca sarvakāryeṣu tripuṇḍraṃ dhārayedbudhaḥ ityuktvā bhagavānbrahmā stutvā devaiḥ samaṃ prabhuḥ  LiP bhasmācchannaiḥ svayaṃ channo virarāma viśāṃpate atha teṣāṃ prasādārthaṃ paśūnāṃ patirīśvaraḥ  LiP sagamaścāṃbayā sārdhaṃ sānnidhyamakarotprabhuḥ atha saṃnihitaṃ rudraṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ surapuṅgavam  LiP rudrādhyāyena sarveśaṃ devadeva mumāpatim devopi devānālokya ghṛṇayā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ  LiP tuṣṭosmītyāha devebhyo varaṃ dātuṃ surārihā  LiP iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāgeṣṭādaśodhyāyaḥśailādiruvācataṃ prabhuṃ prītamanasaṃ praṇipatya vṛṣadhvajam apṛcchanmunayo devāḥ prītikaṇṭakitatvacaḥ  LiP devā ūcuḥbhagavān kena mārgeṇa pūjanīyo dvijātibhiḥ kutra vā kena rūpeṇa vaktumarhasi śaṅkaraḥ  LiP kasyādhikāraḥ pūjāyāṃ brāhmaṇasya kathaṃ prabho kṣatriyāṇāṃ kathaṃ deva vaiśyānāṃ vṛṣabhadhvaja  LiP strīśūdrāṇāṃ kathaṃ vāpi kuṇḍagolādināṃ tu vā hitāya jagatāṃ sarvamasmākaṃ vaktumarhasi  LiP sūta uvācateṣāṃ bhāvaṃ samālokya munīnāṃ nīlalohitaḥ prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā maṇḍalasthaḥ sadāśivaḥ  LiP maṇḍale cāgrato paśyandevadevaṃ sahomayā devāśca munayaḥ sarve vidyutkoṭisamaprabham  LiP aṣṭabāhuṃ caturvaktraṃ dvādaśākṣaṃ mahābhujam
